Article 17: (Approval for Use of Building)
(1) Deleted. <May 8, 2006>
(2) In cases where a client intends to receive approval for the temporary use of the portion of which
construction has been completed before he or she receives a written approval for use under Article 22 (3) 2
of the Act, he or she shall submit an application (including submission in electronic documents) for
approval for temporary use to the permitting authority, as prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land,
Infrastructure and Transport. <Amended on Oct. 29, 2008; Mar. 23, 2013>
(3)  The  permitting  authority  who  has  received  an  application  under  paragraph  (2)  may  approve  a
temporary use only when the portion of which construction has been completed satisfies the standards
under Article 22 (3) 2 of the Act, and with respect to buildings of which construction is completed at the
time when it is inadequate to take necessary measures for landscaping, such as tree-planting, its temporary
use may be approved on the condition that necessary measures are to be taken for landscaping, such as
tree-planting, by the time fixed by the permitting authority. <Amended on Oct. 29, 2008>
(4) The effective period of the approval for temporary use shall be within two years: Provided, That the
permitting authority may extend such period for large buildings, or buildings which take a long time in
construction due to works on rock floors, etc. <Amended on Oct. 29, 2008>
(5) "Contractors of main works prescribed by Presidential Decree" in the latter part of Article 22 (6) of the
Act means a person falling under any of the following subparagraphs: <Amended on Oct. 29, 2008; Feb. 18,
2020; Sep. 12, 2023>
1.  A  construction  business  operator  who  has  registered  a  type  of  business  performing  general
construction works or specialized construction works under Article 9 of the Framework Act on the
Construction Industry and is given a contract for construction work by a project owner;
2. A contractor who performs construction works pursuant to the Electrical Construction Business Act,
the Firefighting System Installation Business Act or the Information and Communications Construction
Business Act.

Article 18: (Preparation of Design Documents)
"Building prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 23 (1) 3 of the Act, means any of the following:
<Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; Feb. 18, 2010; Apr. 10, 2012; Jun. 30, 2016>

and publicly announced by the head of a Si/Gun as they impede regional planning or urban/Gun
planning);
2. Temporary building referred to in any of the subparagraphs of Article 15 (5) and prescribed by a
building ordinance.

(b) When the assembly of the main structural members is completed on every floor;

(a) When the arrangement of reinforcing bars for foundation works is completed;
(b) When the arrangement of reinforcing bars for any of the following members, through which the
load of the upper part of the building is transferred to the lower part structurally different from the
upper part, is completed:

Article 19: (Supervision of Construction Works)

(1) Each project owner shall appoint a project supervisor pursuant to Article 25 (1) of the Act to supervise
the relevant construction works, as follows: <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; Dec. 13, 2010; May 22, 2014; Dec. 11,
2018; Jan. 7, 2020; Sep. 14, 2021; Dec. 28, 2021>
1. In any of the following cases: A certified architect:
(a) When constructing a building that requires building permission under Article 11 of the Act
(excluding buildings subject to notifying as to building construction under Article 14 of the Act);
(b) When remodeling a building referred to in Article 6 (1) 6;
2. When constructing a public-use building: A construction engineering business entity defined in the
Construction Technology Promotion Act (excluding where such business entity is the contractor himself
or herself or an affiliate defined in subparagraph 12 of Article 2 of the Monopoly Regulation and Fair
Trade Act) or a certified architect (limited to where a construction project management engineer is
assigned pursuant to Article 60 of the Enforcement Decree of the Construction Technology Promotion
Act).
(2) Where a project supervisor of a public-use building is appointed under paragraph (1), the standards for
assigning the supervisor and setting supervision fees shall be governed by the Construction Technology
Promotion Act. <Amended on May 22, 2014>
(3) "When the progress of the project reaches the stage prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 25 (6)
of the Act means where the construction (in cases of constructing at least two buildings on one site,
referring to the construction of each building) reaches the stage classified as follows: <Amended on Nov. 28,
2014; May 17, 2016; Feb. 3, 2017; Aug. 6, 2019>
1. Where the relevant building has a reinforced concrete structure, steel-framed reinforced concrete
structure, masonry structure, or reinforced concrete block structure: Any of the following stages:
(a) When the arrangement of reinforcing bars for foundation works is completed;
(b) When the arrangement of roof slab bars is completed;
(c) When the arrangement of upper slab bars is completed at every fifth floor above the ground;
2. Where the relevant building has a steel-framed structure: Any of the following stages:
(a) When the arrangement of reinforcing bars for foundation works is completed;
(b) When the assembly of the steel frames for the roof is completed;
(c) When the assembly of main structural members is completed at every third floor above the ground
or at every 20-meter-height;
3. Where the relevant building has a structure, other than those referred to in subparagraph 1 or 2: A
stage in which the installation of molds or cornerstones for foundation works is completed;
4. Where a building falling under subparagraphs 1 through 3 is a piloti-type building with at least three
floors: Any of the following stages:
(a) When the construction reaches any stage specified in subparagraphs 1 through 3, depending on
the structure of the relevant building;

(b) When the construction reaches the stage specified in Article 18-2 (2) 3 (b).
(4) "Project for the use or of the scale prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 25 (5) of the Act,
means construction works for a building with a total floor area of at least 5,000 square meters. <Amended
on Feb. 3, 2017>
(5) Each project supervisor shall perform supervisory duties at a construction site occasionally or when
necessary; and when supervising the following construction works, he or she shall have at least one
assistant architect in the field of construction and at least one assistant architect in the field of civil
engineering,  electricity,  or  machinery  among  assistant  architects  (including  those  belonging  to
professional engineer offices established under Article 6 of the Professional Engineers Act, or construction
engineering business entities, etc. provided for in the subparagraphs of Article 23 (9) of the Certified
Architects Act, who have acquired technical qualifications in the relevant field under the National
Technical Qualifications Act, or are qualified to perform construction project management under Article 4
of the Enforcement Decree of the Construction Technology Promotion Act; hereinafter the same shall
apply) defined in subparagraph 2 of Article 2 of the Certified Architects Act conduct supervisory duties at
respective construction sites during the entire period of construction and during the period of construction
of the relevant field, respectively. In such cases, the assistant architect shall have at least two years’ work
experience in the design, execution of construction, testing, inspection, construction oversight, supervisory
duties, etc. of construction works in the relevant field: <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; Dec. 13, 2010; Dec. 13,
2010; May 22, 2014; Sep. 22, 2015; Sep. 4, 2018; Jan. 7, 2020; Apr. 21, 2020; Sep. 14, 2021>
1. Construction works for a building with a total floor area of at least 5,000 square meters: Provided,
That excluded herefrom shall be construction works of stables or crop cultivation sheds;
2. Construction works for a building with five consecutive floors (including underground floors) and a
total floor area of at least 3,000 square meters;
3. Construction works for apartment buildings;
4. Construction works for quasi-public-use buildings.
(6) Where a project supervisor supervises a project, which does not fall under the subparagraphs of
paragraph (5), for excavation to a depth of at least 10 meters or for building a retaining wall with a height
of at least five meters (excluding construction of a factory with an aggregate floor area of at least 2,000
square meters in an industrial complex defined in subparagraph 14 of Article 2 of the Industrial Cluster
Development and Factory Establishment Act), he or she shall require at least one assistant architect in the
field of architecture or civil engineering to perform supervisory duties in the construction site during the
relevant construction period. In such cases, the assistant architect shall have at least two years’ experience
in the execution, construction oversight, supervision, etc. of the relevant construction works. <Added on
Apr. 21, 2020; Aug. 10, 2021; Sep. 12, 2023>
(7) A project supervisor shall, in cases prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and
Transport where he or she supervises installation of finishing materials for the building falling under
Article 61: (1) 4, have at least one assistant architect in the field of construction or safety management

conduct supervision at the construction site during the period of installation of finishing materials. In such
cases, an assistant architect shall have at least two years’ experience in the design, execution, test,
inspection, construction oversight, supervision, or other similar activities. <Added on Aug. 10, 2021>
(8) Where a project supervisor has an assistant architect conduct supervision pursuant to paragraphs (5)
through (7), he or she shall have an assistant architect who is not supervising other construction sites or
processes, perform supervisory duties. <Added on Aug. 10, 2021>
(9) Supervisory duties to be performed by project supervisors shall be as follows: <Amended on Mar. 23,
2013; Apr. 21, 2020; Aug. 10, 2021>
1. Verification as to whether the contractor is performing construction works in conformity to design
documents;
2. Verification as to whether the building materials used by the contractor conform to the standards
provided for in relevant statutes or regulations;
3. Other matters prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport concerning the
supervision of construction works.
(10) Each project supervisor who assigns an assistant architect to perform the supervisory duties at a
construction site under paragraphs (5) through (7), shall submit a status report on the posting of assistant
architects to the permitting authority within the period classified follow, as prescribed by Ministerial
Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport: <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013; Nov. 28, 2014; Apr. 21, 2020; Aug.
10, 2021>
1. Where the project supervisor assigns an assistant architect for the first time: Seven days from the
scheduled commencement date (referring to the scheduled commencement date in cases of posting an
assistant architect under paragraph (6) or (7));
2. Where the project supervisor replaces an assistant architect: Within seven days from the date of such
replacement;
3.  Where  the  project  supervisor  withdraws  an  assistant  architect:  Seven  days  from  the  date  of
withdrawal.
(11) Upon receiving a status report on the placement of assistant architects from a project supervisor under
paragraph (10), the permitting authority shall without delay verify the details prescribed by Ministerial
Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, such as whether there is an overlap of assistant architects,
and shall forward it to the Korea Institute of Registered Architects defined in the Certified Architects Act
through a Public Information Sharing Center defined in Article 37 of the Electronic Government Act.
<Amended on Mar. 23, 2013; Apr. 21, 2020; Aug. 10, 2021; Jul. 26, 2022; Sep. 12, 2023>
(12) In receipt of a status report on the placement of assistant architects under paragraph (11), the Korea
Institute of Registered Architects shall manage it, and where it has discovered that an assistant architect is
posted  concurrently  at  least  two  construction  sites,  etc.,  it  shall  without  delay  inform  the  relevant
Mayor/Do Governor, the permitting authority, and any other person prescribed by Ministerial Decree of
Land, Infrastructure and Transport of such fact, etc. <Amended on Dec. 12, 2012; Apr. 21, 2020; Aug. 10, 2021;

Jul. 26, 2022; Sep. 12, 2023>
(13) Except as provided in paragraph 12, matters necessary for managing the status of placement of
assistant architects, etc. shall be prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport.
<Added on Sep. 12, 2023>

Article 19-2: (Buildings for Which Permitting Authority Designates Project Supervisors)
(1)  "Buildings  prescribed  by  Presidential  Decree"  in  the  main  clause,  with  the  exception  of  the
subparagraphs, of Article 25 (2) of the Act, means the following: <Amended on Oct. 24, 2017; Feb. 12, 2019>
1.  Buildings  not  falling  under  any  subparagraph  of  Article  41  (1)  of  the  Framework  Act  on  the
Construction  Industry  that  does  not  fall  under  any  of  the  following  items:
(a) A detached houses referred to in subparagraph 1 (a) of Appendix 1;
(b) A warehouse, storage, workshop, compost shed, stable, and fish farm built for agriculture,
forestry, or livestock industry and other buildings of similar use;
(c)  Where  the  construction  work  of  relevant  buildings  is  minor  in  scale  that  falls  under  any
subparagraph of Article 8 (1) of the Enforcement Decree of the Framework Act on the Construction
Industry;
2. Any of the following buildings used as housing (including where any of the following buildings is
annexed with a building, other than such buildings, into one building):
(a) Apartment houses;
(b) Tenement houses;
(c) Multi-household houses;
(d) Multi-user houses;
(e) Multi-unit houses;
3. Deleted. <Feb. 12, 2019>
(2) To designate a project supervisor pursuant to the main clause, with the exception of the subparagraphs,
of Article 25 (2) of the Act, a Mayor/Do Governor shall prepare and manage a list of project supervisors
after making a recruitment notice to persons classified as follows: In such cases, the Mayor/Do Governor
shall have a prior consultation with the head of a competent Si/Gun/Gu. <Amended on Apr. 21, 2020; Sep. 14,
2021>
1. For a public-use building: A certified architect who has filed a report on the establishment of an
architectural  firm  pursuant  to  Article  23  (1)  of  the  Certified  Architects  Act  and  a  construction
engineering  business  entity  under  the  Construction  Technology  Promotion  Act;

2. In other cases: A certified architect who has filed a report on the establishment of an architectural
firm under Article 23 (1) of the Certified Architects Act.
(3) The client of a building that falls under any subparagraph of paragraph (1), shall file an application for
the designation of a project supervisor with the permitting authority, as prescribed by Ministerial Decree
of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, before filing a report on the commencement of the construction
works under Article 21 of the Act.
(4) The permitting authority shall designate a project supervisor selected from among those on the list
prepared under paragraph (2).
(5) Except as provided in paragraphs (3) and (4), details concerning the recruitment notice of project
supervisors, methods of preparing the list, methods of designating project supervisors, and other relevant
matters, shall be prescribed by ordinance of a City/Do.
(6) "New technology prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 25 (2) 1 of the Act means a new
technology that applies to main structural members of a building and finishing materials of such main
structural members. <Added on Oct. 8, 2020>
(7) "Certified architect prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 25 (2) 2 of the Act means a certified
architect who has won an award or grand prize at a design competition or contest prescribed in any
subparagraph of Article 11 (1) of the Enforcement Decree of the Act on the Promotion of Building Service
Industry over the last 10 years from the date on which the client files an application for the designation of
construction supervision with the permitting authority, under the proviso, with the exception of the
subparagraphs, of that paragraph. <Added on Oct. 8, 2020>
(8) "Relevant contract and other documents prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 25 (13) of the
Act means the following documents: <Added on Feb. 12, 2019; Oct. 8, 2020>
1. A plan for the relevant designer's involvement in the construction process;
2. A contract between the client and the designer.



Article 19-3: (Buildings Subject to Restrictions on Business)
(1) "Major building prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 25-2 (1) of the Act means the following
buildings:
1. Public-use buildings;
2. Quasi-public-use buildings.
(2) "Property damage of at least the scale prescribed by Presidential Decree" in the provisions, with the
exception of the subparagraphs, of Article 25-2 (2) of the Act means property damage, the amount of
which is at least 10/100 of the amount of contract or subcontract and is at least 100 million won.
(3) "Major buildings prescribed by Presidential Decree, such as public use facilities" in the provisions,
with the exception of the subparagraphs, of Article 25-2 (2) of the Act means the following buildings:
1. Public-use buildings;
2. Quasi-public-use buildings.

Article 20: (Agents for On-Site Surveys, Inspections, and Verifications)
(1) The permitting authority may entrust a certified architect to conduct on-site surveys, inspections, and
verifications related to building permission, notifications of building construction, approval for use, and
approval for temporary use of the buildings determined by a building ordinance pursuant to Article 27 (1)
of the Act. In such cases, the permitting authority shall appoint a certified architect to conduct on-site
surveys, inspections, and verifications related to approval for use and approval for temporary use of
buildings as an agent, in compliance with the following requirements: <Amended on Nov. 28, 2014>

1. The architect must be neither the designer nor the project supervisor of the relevant building;
2.  The  permitting  authority  shall  appoint  the  certified  architect  directly,  without  receiving  any
recommendation  from  the  client.
(2) A Mayor/Do Governor shall prepare and manage a list of certified architects who vicariously perform
on-site surveys, inspections, and verifications pursuant to Article 27 (1) of the Act (hereafter in this
Article, referred to as "certified architect to act as proxy") after making a public announcement on
recruitment. In such cases, the Mayor/Do Governor shall have a prior consultation with the head of a
competent Si/Gun/Gu. <Amended on Jan. 8, 2021>
(3) The permitting authority shall designate a certified architect to act as proxy from the list referred to in
paragraph (2). <Added on Jan. 8, 2021>
(4) Matters necessary for public announcement on the recruitment of certified architects to act as proxy
and the preparation and management of the list, and the designation under paragraphs (2) and (3) shall be
prescribed by ordinance of a City/Do. <Added on Jan. 8, 2021>


< 2020. 4. 28.>

Article 21: (Prevention of Harms at Construction Site)
Matters  concerning  the  prevention  of  harms  and  dangers  associated  with  the  construction  or
dismantlement of a building shall comply with the provisions of statutes or regulations pertaining to
industrial safety and health. <Amended on Apr. 28, 2020>

Article 22: (Special Cases concerning Buildings for Public Use)
(1) Where the State or a local government intends to construct a building under Article 29 of the Act, the
head of an administrative agency executing the relevant construction works or a person entrusted with the
execution of such works shall submit (including submission in electronic format) design documents of
such construction works and relevant documents prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure
and Transport to the permitting authority before the commencement of the relevant construction works:
Provided, That the submission of design documents may be omitted where a building important for
national security or treated as national confidential information is constructed. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>
(2) After examining design documents and relevant documents submitted under the main clause of
paragraph (1), the permitting authority shall give notice (including notice in electronic format where the
head of the relevant administrative agency or the entrusted person wishes or design documents, etc. under
paragraph (1) have been submitted in electronic format) of the result of such examination to the head of
the relevant administrative agency or the entrusted person.
(3) The State or a local government shall give notice to the permitting authority of the completion of the
construction of a building under the proviso of Article 29 (3) of the Act, accompanied by relevant
document prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport. <Amended on Mar. 23,
2013>
(4) "Facilities prescribed by Presidential Decree, such as amenities for residents" in the former part of
Article 29: (4) of the Act, means the following: <Added on Jul. 19, 2016>
1. Class 1 neighborhood living facilities;
2. Class 2 neighborhood living facilities (excluding firearm stores, morticians, communal living
facilities, manufacturing stores, public pubs, massage parlors, and singing rooms);
3. Cultural and assembly facilities (limited to performance halls and exhibition halls);
4. Medical facilities;

5. Education and research facilities;
6. Facilities for senior citizens or children;
7. Sports facilities;
8. Business facilities (excluding officetels).


< 2013. 3. 23.>

< 2013. 3. 23.>

Article 22-2: (Computerization of Business of Building Permission)
(1)  A  person  who  intends  to  use  the  data  which  under  the  main  clause,  with  the  exception  of  the
subparagraphs, of Article 32 (2) of the Act with the exception of each subparagraph, have been processed
through the electronic data processing system under paragraph (1) of that Act (hereinafter referred to as
"computerized data") shall submit an application stating the following matters to the head of the relevant
central administrative agency in order to receive an examination by the head of the relevant central
administrative agency:
1. The purpose of and grounds for the use of the computerized data;
2. The scope and contents of the computerized data;
3. The method to be provided with the computerized data;
4. The method of keeping the computerized data, safety control measures, etc.
(2) A person who intends to use computerized data under paragraph (1) shall apply within the minimum
scope satisfying the purpose of the use of the computerized data.
(3)  The  head  of  the  relevant  central  administrative  agency  who  has  received  an  application  under
paragraph (1) shall, after examining the matters in each of the following subparagraphs, inform the
applicant of the result of the examination within 15 days from the date on which he or she received such
application:
1. Feasibility, appropriateness and public nature of the matters in each subparagraph of paragraph (1);
2. Whether or not the standards for protection of personal information under Article 32 (3) of the Act
are satisfied;
3. Whether or not a measure for the prevention of use of computerized data for purposes beyond the
purpose of their use has been formulated.
(4) A person who intends to obtain approval for the use of computerized data under Article 32 (2) of the
Act shall submit to the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, Mayor/Do Governor, or the head of
a Si/Gun/Gu an application for approval for the use of computerized data on architectural administration,
which is prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, attaching thereto the
result  of  examination  under  paragraph  (3):  Provided,  That  in  cases  where  the  head  of  a  central
administrative agency or the head of a local government intends to use computerized data, he or she may
apply for such approval with documents stating the grounds for and purpose of the use of computerized
data, safety control measures, etc. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>
(5) "Guidelines for the protection of personal information of clients and other parties prescribed by
Presidential Decree" in the former part of Article 32 (3) of the Act means the standards in each of the
following:

1. The requested computerized data are not to be information from which certain individual can be
identified through the name, resident registration number, or other description which are included in the
data (including information from which certain individual cannot be identified from the relevant single
information but can be easily identified if combined with other information), or other information that
are likely to disturb the privacy of an individual: Provided, That in cases where there exits the consent
of the individual concerned or grounds in other Acts, the use thereof may be allowed;
2. In cases where computerized data containing personal information are used under the proviso of
subparagraph 1, safety control measures are to be prepared against the use of the computerized data for
purposes, other than their approved purposes, leakage, loss, theft, etc.
(6) The Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, Mayor/Do Governor, or head of a Si/Gun/Gu shall,
when he or she approved the use of computerized data under Article 32 (3) of the Act, record and manage
the details of the approval. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>


< 2013. 3. 23.>

< 2013. 3. 23.>

< 2013. 3. 23., 2019. 8. 6.>

< 2013. 3. 23.>

Article 22-3: (Computerized Data Users Subject to Guidance and Supervision)
(1) Persons subject to guidance for and supervision of the matters concerning the retention or management
of computerized data among persons using computerized data under Article 33 (1) of the Act shall be
those using computerized data (including computerized data provided under other statutes or regulations)

as classified in each of the following subparagraphs: Provided, That the State and local governments shall
be excluded herefrom: <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>
1. The Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport: Persons who use not less than 500,000 cases of
computerized data on a national basis yearly;
2. Mayors/Do Governors: Persons who use not less than 100,000 cases of computerized data on a
City/Do basis yearly;
3. The head of a Si/Gun/Gu: Persons who use not less than 50,000 cases of computerized data on a
Si/Gun/Gu basis yearly.
(2) The Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, Mayor/Do Governor or head of a Si/Gun/Gu may,
if necessary for guidance and supervision under Article 33 (1) of the Act, request a person subject to
guidance and supervision under paragraph (1) to submit the data in each of the following subparagraphs:
<Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>
1. Materials on the status of use of electronic data;
2. Materials on safety management measures to keep step with the use of electronic data;
(3) A person who has been requested to submit data under paragraph (2) shall submit the relevant data
within 15 days unless there is a good reason not to do so.
(4) The Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, Mayor/Do Governor, or head of a Si/Gun/Gu shall,
when intending to conduct an on-site survey of the actual status of use of computerized data under Article
33 (1) of the Act, notify the person subject to investigation of the purpose and details of investigation,
identity of investigators, date of investigation, etc. by not later than seven days before the investigation.
<Amended on Mar. 23, 2013; Aug. 6, 2019>
(5) The Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, Mayor/Do Governor, or head of a Si/Gun/Gu shall
notify the person subject to investigation of the result of the on-site investigation under paragraph (4), and
may request for corrections when necessary as a result of the investigation. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>


< 2014. 10. 14.>

< 2014. 10. 14.>

Article 22-4: (Integrated Civil Service Center for Building Projects)
(1) Every civil service center established under the jurisdiction of each Special Self-Governing City,
Special Self-Governing Province, or Si/Gun/Gu pursuant to Article 34 of the Act, shall perform the
following: <Amended on Oct. 14, 2014>
1. Affairs concerning approval for use under Article 22 of the Act;
2.  Affairs  concerning  building  permission,  approval  for  use,  and  approval  for  temporary  use  of
buildings regarding which a certified architect conducts on-site surveys, inspections, and verifications,
as an agent under Article 27 (1) of the Act;
3. Affairs concerning the preparation and management of the building register;
4. Affairs concerning the handling of complex civil petitions;
5. Consulting on building permission, notifications of building construction, or change of uses of
buildings;
6. Consulting on disputes arising between construction participants;
7. Other affairs deemed necessary for the benefits of residents by the Special Self-Governing City
Mayor, the Special Self-Governing Province Governor, or the head of a Si/ Gun/Gu.
(2) Civil service centers referred to in paragraph (1) shall be established at a place readily accessible by
civil petitioners, and the organization and functions of such center shall be determined by a municipal rule
of each Special Self-Governing City, Special Self-Governing Province, or Si/Gun/Gu. <Amended on Oct.
14, 2014>

Article 24: (Building Instructors)
(1) Building instructors referred to in Article 37 of the Act (hereinafter referred to as “building instructor”)
shall be designated by the Special Self-Governing City Mayor, the Special Self-Governing Province
Governor, or the head of a Si/Gun/Gu from among public officials working in the field of construction in
the Special Self-Governing City, Special Self-Governing Province, or Si/Gun/Gu and persons with
abundant knowledge of construction, who have the qualifications prescribed by a building ordinance.
<Amended on Jul. 19, 2012; Oct. 14, 2014>
(2) The duties of building instructors are as follows:
1. Guidance for buildings under construction after its notification of building construction has been
filed, and verification as to whether construction is illegally conducted, instructions and control;
2. Verification as to whether the site, height and shape, structural safety, fire safety, building service,
etc. of a building are properly maintained and managed in compliance with the provisions of the statutes
or regulations, etc. instructions and control;
3. Control of buildings built or, the use of which has been changed, without obtaining permission or
filing a report.
(3) Every building instructor who performs the duties under paragraph (2) shall carry a certificate
indicating his or her authority and present it to relevant persons.
(4) Procedures for designating building instructors, standards for remuneration, and other necessary
matters, shall be determined by a building ordinance.


< 2012. 7. 19., 2013. 3. 23.>


Article 25: (Building Register)
"Circumstances prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 38 (1) 4 of the Act, means any of the
following circumstances: <Amended on Jul. 19, 2012; Mar. 23, 2013>
1. Where an application for the initial registration on the building register or registration of alteration is
filed under Articles 56 and 57 of the Act on Ownership and Management of Condominium Buildings;

2.  Where  the  owner  of  a  building  constructed,  maintained  and  managed  in  compliance  with  the
provisions of the statutes or regulations, etc. before the Act enters into force files an application for
transcription of the management ledger of the relevant building or other public books similar thereto
into the building register under Article 38 of the Act;
3. Other circumstances prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, where it
is necessary to alter the entered matters.

Article 27: (Landscaping of Sites)
(1) Measures, such as landscaping, need not be taken for any of the following buildings, pursuant to the
proviso of Article 42 (1) of the Act: <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; Dec. 13, 2010; Apr. 10, 2012; Dec. 12, 2012;
Mar. 23, 2013>
1. A building constructed in a green area;
2. A factory constructed on a site not exceeding 5,000 square meters;
3. A factory with a total floor area not exceeding 1,500 square meters;
4. A factory in an industrial complex defined in subparagraph 14 of Article 2 of the Industrial Cluster
Development and Factory Establishment Act;
5. A building determined by a building ordinance, falling under cases where its site contains salt, or
where it is impractical or irrational to take measures, such as landscaping, in consideration of the
characteristics of its use;
6. A stable;
7. A temporary building referred to in Article 20 (1) of the Act;
8. A logistics facility with a total floor area not exceeding 1,500 square meters (excluding those
constructed  in  residential  areas  or  commercial  areas)  prescribed  by  Ministerial  Decree  of  Land,
Infrastructure  and  Transport;

9. A building in a natural environment conservation area, an agricultural and forestry area, or a
management area (excluding the areas designated as district unit planning zones) designated under the
National Land Planning and Utilization Act;
10. Any of the following buildings prescribed by a building ordinance:
(a) Tourist facilities established in a tourist destination defined in subparagraph 6 of Article 2 of the
Tourism Promotion Act or a tourist complex defined in subparagraph 7 of that Article;
(b) Facilities for a specialized resort business defined in Article 2 (1) 3 (a) of the Enforcement Decree
of the Tourism Promotion Act or facilities for a general resort complex business defined in Article 2
(1) 3 (b) of that Enforcement Decree;
(c) Tourist facilities established in a tourism and resort type district-unit planning zone referred to in
subparagraph  10  of  Article  48  of  the  Enforcement  Decree  of  the  National  Land  Planning  and
Utilization  Act;
(d) Golf courses referred to in Appendix 1 of the Enforcement Decree of the Installation and
Utilization of Sports Facilities Act.
(2) The standards for measures, such as landscaping, under the proviso of Article 42 (1) of the Act, shall
be as prescribed in each of the following: Provided, That where more lenient standards than any of the
following have been otherwise provided for by a building ordinance, such lenient standards shall prevail:
<Amended on Sep. 9, 2009; Mar. 29, 2017; Mar. 12, 2019>
1. Factories (excluding factories referred to in paragraph (1) 2 through 4) and logistics facilities
(excluding logistics facilities referred to in paragraph (1) 8 and logistics facilities constructed in
residential areas or commercial areas):
(a) Where the total floor area exceeds 2,000 square meters: More than 10 percent of the site area;
(b) Where the total floor area exceeds 1,500 square meters but does not exceed 2,000 square meters:
More than five percent of the site area;
2. Airport facilities defined in subparagraph 7 of Article 2 of the Airport Facilities Act: More than 10
percent of the site area (excluding the area used for aircraft take-off and landing facilities, such as
runways, taxiways, aprons, and landing zones);
3. Station facilities which is part of the railroad defined in subparagraph 1 of Article 2 of the Act on
Railroad Construction and Railroad Facilities Management: More than 10 percent of the site area
(excluding the area used for facilities for railroad operations, such as railroad tracks and platforms);
4. Other buildings built on a site, which exceeds 200 square meters but does not exceed 300 square
meters: More than 10 percent of the site area.
(3) Where the rooftop of a building is landscaped or other necessary measures are taken for the rooftop of
a building in conformity to the standards publicly notified by the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and
Transport under Article 42 (2) of the Act, an area equivalent to 2/3 of the landscaped area of the rooftop
may be calculated as a site area subject to landscaping under Article 42 (1) of the Act. In such cases, the
area to be calculated as an area subject to landscaping shall not exceed 50/100 of the area subject to

landscaping under Article 42 (1) of the Act. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>

Article 27-2: (Securing Privately-Owned Public Space)
(1) A privately-owned public space or privately-owned public open space (hereafter in this Article referred
to as “POPS, etc.”) shall be established on the site of any of the following buildings pursuant to Article 43
(1) of the Act. In such cases, the privately-owned public space may have a piloti structure: <Amended on
Jul. 16, 2009; Nov. 20, 2013; Oct. 22, 2019>
1. Cultural or assembly facilities, religious facilities, sales facilities (excluding distribution facilities for
agricultural and fishery products established under the Act on Distribution and Price Stabilization of
Agricultural and Fishery Products), transportation facilities (limited to passenger facilities), business
facilities, or lodging facilities with a total floor area of at least 5,000 square meters for the relevant use;
2. Other public-use facilities, which are buildings determined by a building ordinance.
(2) The area of a POPS, etc. shall be prescribed by a building ordinance, within 10 percent of the area of
the relevant site. In such cases, the landscaping area under Article 42 of the Act and the area for taking a
measure for preserving buried cultural heritage at site under Article 14 (1) 1 of the Act on Protection and
Inspection of Buried Cultural Heritage may be included in a POPS, etc. <Amended on Nov. 11, 2011; Aug. 3,
2015; Jun. 27, 2017>
(3) When a POPS, etc. is established pursuant to paragraph (1), facilities prescribed by a building
ordinance, such as benches or landscaping facilities, shall be installed so that all people may use them at
their convenience in an environmentally friendly manner. <Amended on Oct. 22, 2019>
(4) Where a POPS, etc. is established in a building referred to in paragraph (1) (including where a building
referred to in paragraph (1) and another building not falling under paragraph (1), are consolidated into one
building), Articles 56 and 60 of the Act shall be relaxed according to the ratio of the scale of the POPS,
etc. to the scale of the site within the following ratios, pursuant to Article 43 (2) of the Act: Provided, That
where the ratios determined by a building ordinance within the following ratios, exceeds the relaxed ratio,
such ratios determined by a building ordinance shall apply: <Amended on Nov. 11, 2014>
1. The floor area ratio provided for in Article 56 of the Act shall not exceed 1.2 times the floor area ratio
applicable to the relevant area;
2. The height limit set under Article 60 of the Act shall not exceed 1.2 times the height limit applicable
to the relevant building.
(5) Paragraph (4) shall apply mutatis mutandis where a POPS, etc., which complies with Article 43 (4) of
the Act and paragraphs (2) and (3) of this Article is established on the site of a building (excluding multi-
family housing other than cases of building housing units and non-housing units in the shape of the same
building, among multi-family housing units subject to approval of the business plan under Article 15 (1)
of the Housing Act) unnecessary to secure a POPS, etc. therein. <Amended on Nov. 11, 2014; Aug. 11, 2016;
Jan. 20, 2017; Oct. 22, 2019>

(6) Cultural or promotional events for residents may be held in a POPS, etc. for up to 60 days annually, as
prescribed by a building ordinance: Provided, That it is prohibited to engage in any activity obstructing the
public use of the relevant POPS, etc., such as installing a fence. <Added on Jun. 30, 2009>
(7) The activities restricted pursuant to Article 43 (4) of the Act shall be as follows: <Added on Apr. 21,
2020>
1. Occupying a specific space in a POPS, etc. to run business;
2. The following acts that obstruct the use of a POPS, etc.:
(a) Installing any facility other than facilities referred to in paragraph (3) in the POPS, etc.;
(b) Storing materials in the POPS, etc.;
3. Blocking the entry into a POPS, etc., such as installing a fence or a wall, or closing an entrance;
4. Damaging a POPS, etc. and amenities installed therein;
5. Other acts specified by a building ordinance as similar to the activities referred to in subparagraphs 1
through 4.


< 2009. 6. 30.,
2009. 7. 16.>

Article 28: (Relationship between Site and Road)
(1) "Vacant lot prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 44 (1) 2 of the Act, means a plaza, park,
amusement park, and other open areas recognized by the permitting authority, in which construction is
prohibited under relevant statutes or regulations and no obstruction to the traffic of the general public
exists.
(2) The site of a building (excluding a stable, crop cultivation shed, or other similar building in the scale
prescribed by a building ordinance) with a total floor area exceeding 2,000 square meters (in cases of
factories, 3,000 square meters) shall face at least four meters a road, which is at least six meters wide
under Article 44 (2) of the Act. <Amended on Jun. 30, 2009; Jul. 16, 2009>

intersecting  road  right-of-way  lines,  which  points  are  located  at  the  following  distance  from  the
intersection  of  said  right-of-way  lines,  as  shown  in  Appendix  below:
(2) Pursuant to Article 46 (2) of the Act, the Special Self-Governing City Mayor, the Special Self-
Governing Province Governor, or the head of a Si/Gun/Gu may separately designate building lines within
four meters in urban areas designated under Article 36 (1) 1 of the National Land Planning and Utilization
Act. <Amended on Oct. 14, 2014>

head of a Si/Gun/Gu intends to designate the building lines under paragraph (2), he or she shall publicly
announce the details thereof in the public gazette of the relevant local government, daily newspapers, web-
sites, etc. for at least 30 days in advance, and a person who has opinions on the details of the public
announcement may submit (including submission by electronic documents) his or her opinions to the
Special Self-Governing City Mayor, the Special Self-Governing Province Governor, or the head of the
Si/Gun/Gu within the period for such public announcement. <Amended on Oct. 14, 2014>

Article 32: (Verification of Structural Safety)
(1) To construct or substantially repair a building under Article 11 (1) of the Act, the designer of the
building shall verify its structural safety in accordance with the structural standards, etc. prescribed by

Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, pursuant to Article 48 (2): <Amended on Jul. 16,
2009; Mar. 23, 2013; May 31, 2013; Nov. 28, 2014>
1. Deleted; <Nov. 28, 2014>
2. Deleted. <Nov. 28, 2014>
3. Deleted. <Nov. 28, 2014>
4. Deleted. <Nov. 28, 2014>
5. Deleted. <Nov. 28, 2014>
6. Deleted. <Nov. 28, 2014>
7. Deleted. <Nov. 28, 2014>
(2) The client of any of the following buildings among buildings, the structural safety of which has been
verified pursuant to paragraph (1), shall receive the documents certifying the structural safety of the
relevant building from the designer of such building, and shall submit such documents to the permitting
authority when filing a report on the commencement of the construction works under Article 21 of the
Act: Provided, That the same shall not apply to buildings constructed in conformity to the standard design
documents: <Amended on Nov. 28, 2014; Sep. 22, 2015; Feb. 3, 2017; Oct. 24, 2017; Dec. 4, 2018>
1. A building with at least two floors [three floors in the case of a wooden structure building built with main
structural members including columns and beams made of wood (hereinafter referred to as "wooden structure
building")];
2. A building with a total floor area of at least 200 square meters (500 square meters for a wooden
structure building): Provided, That excluded herefrom shall be warehouses, cattle sheds, and crop
cultivation sheds;
3. A building at least 13 meters tall;
4. A building, the eaves of which are at least nine meters tall;
5. A building, the distance between pillars of which is at least 10 meters;
6. A building with great significance in terms of use and scale, which is prescribed by Ministerial
Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport;
7. A building prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, worth preserving
as national cultural heritage;
8. A building referred to in subparagraph 18 (a) or (c) of Article 2;
9. A detached house referred to in subparagraph 1 of Appendix 1 and multi-family housing referred to
in subparagraph 2 of that Table.
(3) A client who intends to conduct construction works or substantial repair of an existing building
pursuant to Article 6 (1) 6 (c), shall submit documents certifying the structural safety to the permitting
authority when he or she requests the criteria to be applied leniently pursuant to Article 5 (1) of the Act.
<Added on Feb. 3, 2017>



Article 32-2: (Disclosure of Seismic Capacity of Buildings)
(1)  "Any  building  prescribed  by  Presidential  Decree"  in  the  proviso,  with  the  exception  of  the
subparagraphs,  of  Article  48-3  (1)  of  the  Act  means  any  of  the  following  buildings:
1. A warehouse, a cattle shed, a crop cultivation shed, or a building constructed in compliance with the
standard design documents, which does not fall under any subparagraph of Article 32 (2) 1, or 3 through
9;
2. A building to which structural standards for small buildings prescribed by Ministerial Decree of
Land, Infrastructure and Transport applies, among the structural standards referred to in Article 32 (1).
(2) "Building prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 48-3 (1) 3 of the Act means a building
specified in any subparagraph of Article 32 (2) 3 through 9.

Article 34: (Installation of Direct Stairs)
(1) On each floor of a building, direct stairs leading to the refuge floor or the ground floor (including
ramps; hereinafter the same shall apply) other than the refuge floor (referring to a floor having a doorway
leading directly to the ground floor and the refuge area of a skyscraper under paragraphs (3) and (4);
hereinafter the same shall apply) shall be installed so the walking distance from any point in the living
room to the stairs (referring to one staircase nearest to the living room) does not exceed 30 meters:

Provided, That in cases of a building main structural members of which (excluding a performance hall,
assembly hall, auditorium and exhibition hall which are installed on underground floors and which have a
total floor area exceeding 300 square meters) has a fire-resistant structure or are made of noncombustible
materials, the walking distance shall not exceed 50 meters (or 40 meters for the 16th floor or above in
cases of multi-family housing with at least 16 floors), and in cases of a factory prescribed by Ministerial
Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, which is equipped with automatic fire extinguishers, such as
sprinklers, in an automated production facility, the walking distance shall not exceed 75 meters (100
meters in cases of unmanned factories). <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; Feb. 18, 2010; Dec. 30, 2011; Mar. 23,
2013; Aug. 6, 2019; Oct. 8, 2020>
(2) In a building in which any floor, other than the refuge floor, is for a use and in a scale falling under any
of the following, at least two direct staircases leading to the refuge floor or to the ground floor shall be
installed pursuant to Article 49 (1) of the Act, in conformity to the standards prescribed by Ministerial
Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport: <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; Mar. 23, 2013; Mar. 24, 2014; Sep.
22, 2015; Feb. 3, 2017>
1. A floor used for performance halls or religious assembly facilities among Class 2 neighborhood
living facilities, or cultural and assembly facilities (excluding exhibition halls, and zoological and
botanical gardens), or religious facilities or bar business among amusement facilities, or funeral
facilities, the total floor area of which used for relevant purposes is at least 200 square meters (300
square  meters  in  cases  of  performance  halls  and  religious  assembly  facilities  among  Class  2
neighborhood  living  facilities);
2. A third or upper floor used for multi-user houses or multi-unit houses among detached houses,
neuropsychiatric clinics (limited to those having patent rooms) among Class 1 neighborhood living
facilities, Internet computer game facilities (applicable only where the total floor area used for the
relevant purpose is at least 300 square meters) or private teaching institutes or reading rooms, sales
facilities, and transportation facilities (limited to passenger facilities) among Class 2 neighborhood
living facilities, medical facilities (excluding dental clinics having no inpatient rooms), private teaching
institutes among education and research facilities, children-related facilities, welfare facilities for senior
citizens, and residential homes for persons with disabilities (referring to the facilities prescribed by
Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport among residential homes for persons with
disabilities referred to in Article 58 (1) 1 of the Act on Welfare of Persons with Disabilities; hereinafter
the same shall apply), medical rehabilitation facilities for persons with disabilities referred to in Article
58  (1)  4  of  the  Act  on  Welfare  of  Persons  with  Disabilities  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  "medical
rehabilitation facilities for persons with disabilities“) among facilities for senior citizens and children, or
youth hostels among training facilities, or lodging facilities, the total floor area of the living room on
which used for relevant purposes is at least 200 square meters;
3. A floor used for multi-family housing (excluding those which have not more than four dwelling units
on each floor) or officetels among business facilities, on which the total floor area of the living room on

which used for relevant purposes is at least 300 square meters;
4. A third or upper floor not used for any of the purposes prescribed in subparagraphs 1 through 3, the
total floor area of the living room on which is at least 400 square meters;
5. An underground floor the total floor area of the living room on which is at least 200 square meters.
(3) In each skyscraper, a refuge area (referring to a refuge area established on the middle floor of a
building for the purpose of escape or safety; hereinafter the same shall apply) directly connected to the
direct staircase leading to the refuge floor or the ground floor shall be established on a maximum of 30
floors each from the ground floor. <Added on Jul. 16, 2009; Dec. 30, 2011>
(4) In each quasi-skyscrapers, at least one refuge area directly connected to the direct staircase leading to
the refuge floor or the ground floor shall be established on a floor located within five floors above and
below the floor corresponding to a half of total number of floors of the building: Provided, That this shall
not apply where direct staircases leading to the refuge floor or the ground floor are to be established in
conformity to the standards prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport.
<Added on Dec. 30, 2011; Mar. 23, 2013>
(5) The size and criteria for the establishment of refuge areas under paragraphs (3) and (4) shall be
prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport. <Added on Jul. 16, 2009; Dec. 30,
2011; Mar. 23, 2013>

Article 35: (Installation of Fire Escape Stairs)
(1) Direct stairs installed on the fifth or upper floor or the second or lower underground floor pursuant to
Article 49: (1) of the Act, shall be installed as fire escape stairs or special escape stairs in accordance with
the standards prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport: Provided, That the
same shall not apply where main structural members have a fire-resistant structure or are made of
noncombustible materials and either of the following is applicable: <Amended on Oct. 29, 2008; Mar. 23,
2013>
1. Where the total floor area of the fifth or upper floor does not exceed 200 square meters;
2. Where a fire compartment is installed for every 200 or fewer square meters of floor area of the fifth
or upper floor.
(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), direct stairs leading to the refuge floor or to the ground from the 11th
(16th, in cases of multi-family housing) or upper floors (excluding floors with a floor area of less than 400
square meters) or from the third or lower underground floors (excluding floors with a floor area of less
than 400 square meters) of a building (excluding side corridor-type multi-family housing) shall be
installed as special escape stairs.  <Amended  on  Oct.  29,  2008>
(3) At least one direct staircases installed on the floor used for sales facilities under paragraph (1) shall be
special escape stairs. <Amended on Oct. 29, 2008>
(4) Deleted. <Dec. 30, 1995>
(5) On the fifth or upper floor used for exhibition halls, or zoological or botanical gardens among cultural
and assembly facilities, sales facilities, transportation facilities (limited to passenger facilities), sports
facilities, amusement facilities, tourist resting facilities (limited to those used by the general public), or
training facilities in living zones among training facilities, on which the total floor area used for relevant
purposes exceeds 2,000 square meters, one escape staircase or special escape staircase (limited to fire
escape stairs or special escape stairs out of use on the fourth or lower floor), other than direct stairs
installed under Article 34, shall be installed for every excess 2,000 square meters. <Amended on Oct. 29,
2008; Jul. 16, 2009>
(6) Deleted. <Apr. 30, 1999>


< 2014. 3. 24.>


Article 36: (Installation of Outdoor Escape Stairs)
On the third floor or upper floor (excluding refuge floors) of a building, which is used for any of the
following purposes, outdoor escape stairs leading to the ground from the floor concerned, other than direct
stairs under Article 34, shall be separately installed: <Amended on Mar. 24, 2014>
1. It is to be a floor used for a performance hall among performance halls (applicable only where the
total floor area used for the relevant purpose is at least 300 square meters) among Class 2 neighborhood
living facilities, performance hall among cultural and assembly facilities, or a bar business among
amusement facilities, on which the total floor area of the living room is at least 300 square meters;
2. It is to be a floor used for an assembly hall among cultural and assembly facilities, on which the total
floor area of the living room is at least 1,000 square meters.



Article 37: (Installation of Open Space between Underground Floor and Refuge Floor)
In cases of installing a performance hall, assembly hall, auditorium, or exhibition hall which has a total
floor area of not less than 3,000 square meters on underground floor, an outside space with an open ceiling
shall be installed so as to make those in each room able to escape from each underground floor to the
outside of the building and evacuate to the refuge floor via outside stairs or ramps.


< 2013. 3. 23., 2014. 3. 24., 2017.
2. 3., 2019. 8. 6.>


Article 38: (Installation of Exits from Auditoriums)
Under Article 49 (1) of the Act, exits from the auditorium or assembly room shall be installed in any of
the following buildings according to the standards prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure
and Transport: <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013; Mar. 24, 2014; Feb. 3, 2017; Aug. 6, 2019>
1. Performance halls and religious assembly facilities (applicable only where the total floor area used
for the relevant purpose is at least 300 square meters, respectively) among Class 2 neighborhood living
facilities;
2. Cultural and assembly facilities (excluding exhibition halls, and zoological and botanical gardens);
3. Religious facilities;
4. Amusement facilities;
5. Funeral facilities.

2014. 3. 24., 2017. 2. 3.>

< 2013. 3. 23.>

Article 39: (Installation of Exit to Outside of Buildings)
(1) Under Article 49 (1) of the Act, exits leading from the inside of a building to the outside shall be
installed in a building falling under any of the following according to the standards prescribed by
Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport: <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013; Mar. 24, 2014; Feb. 3,
2017>

1. Performance halls, religious assembly facilities, and Internet computer game providing facilities
(applicable only where the total floor area used for the relevant purpose is at least 300 square meters,
respectively) among Class 2 neighborhood living facilities;
2. Cultural and assembly facilities (excluding exhibition halls, and zoological and botanical gardens);
3. Religious facilities;
4. Sales facilities;
5. Office buildings of the State or a local government among business facilities;
6. Amusement facilities;
7. Warehouse facilities, the total floor area of which is at least 5,000 square meters;
8. Schools among education and research facilities;
9. Funeral facilities;
10. Buildings in which elevators are to be installed.
(2) A revolving door to be installed at the entrance of a building under Article 49 (1) of the Act shall be in
conformity to the standards prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport.
<Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>

Article 40: (Installation of Rooftop Plaza)
(1) A rail at least 1.2 meters high shall be installed around a rooftop plaza, balcony, etc. (referring to a
balcony or others similar thereto) on the second or upper floor: Provided, That the same shall not apply in
cases of structures not allowing access to such balcony, etc. <Amended on Sep. 4, 2018>
(2) Where the fifth or upper floor is used for performance halls, religious assembly facilities, and Internet
computer game providing facilities (applicable only where the total floor area used for the relevant
purpose is at least 300 square meters, respectively) among Class 2 neighborhood living facilities, cultural
and assembly facilities (excluding exhibition halls, and zoological and botanical gardens), religious
facilities, sales facilities, bar business among amusement facilities, or funeral facilities, a plaza which may
be used for the purpose of escape shall be installed on the roof. <Amended on Mar. 24, 2014; Feb. 3, 2017>
(3) Any of the following buildings shall be equipped with an automatic emergency door opener and closer
(referring to a device interworking with a fire-fighting system, which automatically releases the locked
state in case of emergency such as fire) which has obtained performance certification under Article 40 (1)
of the Act on Installation and Management of Firefighting Systems and received a product inspection
under paragraph (2) of that Article: <Added on Jan. 8, 2021; Nov. 29, 2022>
1. A building which requires the installation of a rooftop plaza which can be used for evacuation under
paragraph (2);
2.  The  following  buildings  requiring  the  installation  of  a  rooftop  plaza  which  can  be  used  for
evacuation:
(a) A public-use building;
(b) A multi-family housing with a total floor area of at least 1,000 square meters.
(4) On the roof of a building which has at least 11 floors and the total floor area of the 11th and upper
floors of which is not less than 10,000 square meters, the space as classified in the following shall be
secured: <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; Dec. 30, 2011; Jan. 8, 2021>
1. Where the roof of the building is a flat type: A space for installation of a heliport or for saving human
lives, etc. by a helicopter;
2. Where the roof of the building is a sloping type: A refuge area installed beneath the sloping roof.
(5) The standards for securing the space for installation of a heliport or for saving human lives, etc. by a
helicopter and for installation of the refuge area beneath a sloping roof under paragraph (4) shall be
prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport. <Added on Dec. 30, 2011; Mar. 23,

2013; Jan. 8, 2021>


< 2010. 12. 13., 2015. 9. 22., 2016. 5. 17., 2017. 2. 3.>

< 2010. 12. 13., 2011. 12. 30., 2015. 9. 22.>

Article 41: (Installation of Passage Necessary for Escape and Firefighting within Sites)
(1) Within the site of a building, a passage leading to a road or an open space (referring to a park, plaza
and others similar thereto, which do not hinder access to the relevant site for the purpose of escape and
firefighting; hereafter in this Article the same shall apply) from the main entrance leading to the outside of
the building, and escape stairs leading to the ground floor and special escape stairs shall be installed in
accordance with each of the following criteria: <Amended on Dec. 13, 2010; Sep. 22, 2015; May 17, 2016; Feb.
3, 2017>
1. The width of the passage shall be secured in compliance with the standards classified as follows:
(a) Detached houses: The effective width shall be at least 0.9 meter;
(b) Cultural and assembly facilities, religious facilities, medical facilities, amusement facilities, or
funeral facilities which have a total floor area of at least 500 square meters: The effective width shall
be at least three meters;
(c) Buildings used for other purposes: The effective width shall be at least 1.5 meters;
2. Where the length of the passage inside a piloti is at least two meters, passage-protecting facilities,
such as stakes for preventing entry of motor vehicles, shall be put up or different levels of steps shall be

installed to prevent any hindrance to escape and firefighting.
(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), within a site where a public-use building, quasi-public-use building,
and building with at least 11 floors is constructed, passages through which all the public-use building,
quasi-public-use building, and building with at least 11 floors therein are accessible by fire engines under
Article 21: (hereinafter referred to as "fire engines") of the Framework Act on Fire Services shall be
installed: Provided, That this shall not apply where all the public-use building, quasi-public-use building,
and building with at least 11 floors are constructed directly adjacent to roads or vacant lots where fire
engines can get access, enabling the fire engines to engage in firefighting activities directly from such
roads or vacant lots. <Added on Dec. 13, 2010; Dec. 30, 2011; Sep. 22, 2015>

Article 44: (Applicability to Evacuation Provisions)
In cases where a building is partitioned with floors or walls having a fire-resistant structure without
windows, doorways or other openings (hereinafter referred to as "windows, etc."), each partitioned part
shall be deemed an independent building for purposes of Articles 34 through 41 and 48. <Amended on Sep.
4, 2018>

Article 46: (Installation of Fire Compartments)
(1) In accordance with the main clause of Article 49 (2) of the Act, a building, the main structural
members of which are of a fire-resistant structure or non-combustible materials, with a total floor area
exceeding 1,000 square meters, shall be partitioned with the following structures (hereinafter referred to as
"fire  compartment")  in  accordance  with  the  standards  prescribed  by  Ministerial  Decree  of  Land,
Infrastructure  and  Transport:  Provided,  That  the  nuclear  reactors  and  relevant  facilities  under
subparagraphs 8 and 10 of Article 2 of the Nuclear Safety Act shall be governed by that Act: <Amended on
Oct. 8, 2020; Apr. 29, 2022>
1. Fire-resistant floor and walls;
2. Fire doors or automatic fire shutters under Article 64 (1) 1 or 2 (which meet the standards prescribed
by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport; hereinafter the same shall apply).
(2) Paragraph (1) need not apply to part of any of the following buildings, or the provision therein may be
relaxed for application to the extent not impeding its use: <Amended on Feb. 18, 2010; Feb. 3, 2017; Aug. 6,
2019; Oct. 8, 2020; Apr. 29, 2022; May 15, 2023>

1. An essential part of a living room used for cultural and assembly facilities (excluding zoological and
botanical gardens), religious facilities, sports facilities, or funeral facilities to ensure an unobstructed
line-of-sight and activity space;
2. An essential part for the installation of stationary large machinery or equipment necessary for
manufacturing, processing, transportation, etc. of goods (excluding storage of goods): Provided, That in
cases of the underground floor, it shall be limited to where pedestrians are allowed to pass through and
cars are allowed to enter and exit, as the whole area of one side (referring to the side comprised of at
least 1/4 of the area of exterior walls from the surface side of the underground floor to the side below
the surface of the ground floor) of the exterior wall of the underground floor is open to outside areas;
3. The staircase and corridor, or the platform and shaft of the elevator, which are separated from other
parts of the building by fire compartments: Provided, That the parts where pipes or the like pass through
their floor shall be excluded herefrom;
4. Part of the top floor or refuge floor of a building, which is used for a large conference hall, lecture
hall, sky-lounge, lobby, or refuge area, and essential for such purposes;
5. The floor between dwelling units on two different floors in duplex multi-family housing;
6. A parking lot, the main structural members of which have a fire-resistant structure or are made of
noncombustible materials;
7. Buildings used for detached houses, animal- or plant-related facilities, or defense or military facilities
among correctional and military facilities (limited to facilities used for assemblies, sports, warehouses,
etc.);
8. Parts of the first floor and second floor of a building used for the same purpose are separated from the
other parts of the building by fire compartments (limited to where the total floor area does not exceed
500 square meters).
(3) Where part of the main structural members of a building have a fire-resistant structure or paragraph (1)
is applied leniently regarding part of a building pursuant to paragraph (2), such part with a fire-resistant
structure or the part to which paragraph (1) has been applied leniently, shall be separated from the other
parts by fire compartments. <Amended on Sep. 4, 2018>
(4) In cases of apartments among multi-family housing, in which each dwelling unit on the fourth or upper
floor has no access to at least two direct staircases, at least one refuge area satisfying all of the following
requirements shall be installed in the balcony (including cases where such area adjoins the exterior of the
balcony), jointly with the neighboring dwelling units, or by each dwelling unit. In such cases, the refuge
area installed jointly with the neighboring dwelling units, shall be preferentially installed in a place
accessible to at least two direct staircases through the neighboring dwelling units: <Amended on Mar. 23,
2013; Oct. 8, 2020; Sep. 12, 2023>
1. The refuge area shall have contact with the air outside;
2. The refuge area shall be separated from other indoor areas by fire compartments;

3. The floor area of the refuge area shall be at least three square meters if installed jointly with the
neighboring dwelling units, and at least two square meters if installed by each dwelling unit;
4. The refuge area shall meet the criteria prescribed by the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and
Transport.
(5) Notwithstanding paragraph (4), a refuge area need not be installed if any of the following structures or
facilities is installed in the balcony (in cases of subparagraph 4, including cases where such structure or
facility  adjoins  the  exterior  of  the  balcony)  on  the  fourth  or  upper  floor  of  an  apartment  building:
<Amended  on  Feb.  18,  2010;  Mar.  23,  2013;  Aug.  27,  2014;  Sep.  4,  2018;  Aug.  10,  2021;  Sep.  12,  2023>
1. Where the party wall installed on the balcony to separate from the neighboring dwelling units is an
easily demolishable lightweight structure;
2. Where an emergency exit has been installed on the party wall of the balcony;
3. Where a top-down emergency exit prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and
Transport has been installed on the floor of the balcony;
4. Where the balcony has a structure or facility recognized as having functions equivalent to or better
than a refuge area referred to paragraph (4), as publicly notified by the Minister of Land, Infrastructure
and Transport (hereafter in this subparagraph referred to as "alternative facility"). In such cases, the
Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport shall publicly notify the performance of such alternate
facility,  subject  to  technical  review  from  the  Korea  Institute  of  Civil  Engineering  and  Building
Technology established under Article 8 (1) of the Act on the Establishment, Operation and Fostering of
Government-Funded Science and Technology Research Institutes.
(6)  Any  of  the  following  facilities  shall  be  installed  at  each  floor,  other  than  the  refuge  floors  of
convalescent hospitals, psychiatric hospitals, sanatoriums for senior citizens referred to in Article 34 (1) 1
of  the  Welfare  of  Older  Persons  Act  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  "sanatoriums  for  senior  citizens"),
residential homes for persons with disabilities, and medical rehabilitation facilities for persons with
disabilities: <Added on Sep. 22, 2015; Sep. 4, 2018>
1. A refuge area with separate fire compartments on each floor;
2. A balcony, etc. connected to the living room;
3. A ramp leading to the ground outside the building, or a connecting corridor or passage installed to
allow people to escape to an adjacent building without using a staircase.
(7) "Building for which its use and scale are prescribed by Presidential Decree, such as a large-scale
warehouse" in the proviso of Article 49 (2) of the Act means a warehouse that has a part classified under
paragraph (2) 2 to which paragraph (1) is not applicable or is relaxed for application. <Added on Apr. 29,
2022>


< 2009. 7. 16., 2013. 3. 23., 2016. 1. 19., 2016. 7. 19., 2017. 2. 3., 2018. 2. 9.,
2022. 4. 29.>

< 2009. 7. 16., 2010. 8. 17., 2012. 12. 12., 2014. 3. 24., 2022. 4. 29.>


Article 47: (Restrictions on Uses Impeding Fire Prevention)
(1) Pursuant to the main clause of Article 49 (2) of the Act, medical facilities, facilities for senior citizens
and children (limited to children-related facilities and welfare facilities for senior citizens), multi-family
housing, funeral facilities or Class 1 neighborhood living facilities (applicable only to postpartum care
centers) shall not be installed in a building where amusement facilities, storage and treatment facilities for
hazardous substances, factories or motor vehicle-related facilities (limited to repair shops) are installed:
Provided, That the those facilities may be installed together in the same building in the following cases, as
prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport: <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; Mar. 23,
2013; Jan. 19, 2016; Jul. 19, 2016; Feb. 3, 2017; Feb. 9, 2018; Apr. 29, 2022>
1. Where multi-family housing (limited to a dormitory) and a factory are located in the same building;
2. Where a redevelopment project is implemented in a central commercial area, general commercial
area, or neighboring commercial area designated under the Act on the Improvement of Urban Areas and
Residential Environments;
3. Where multi-family housing and a recreational facility are located in the same skyscraper: Provided,
That the doorway, stairs, and elevator of a house shall be structured detached to facilities, other than the
house, for the purposes of protecting privacy, securing living security, such as preventing fire and
crime, and protecting living environments from noise, offensive odor, etc.;
4. Where a knowledge industry center defined in subparagraph 13 of Article 2 of the Industrial Cluster
Development  and  Factory  Establishment  Act  and  a  workplace  child-care  center  referred  to  in

subparagraph 4 of Article 10 of the Infant Care Act are located in the same building.
(2) Pursuant to the main clause of Article 49 (2) of the Act, a facility used for any of the following
purposes shall not be installed together in the same building: <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; Aug. 17, 2010; Dec.
12, 2012; Mar. 24, 2014; Apr. 29, 2022>
1. Children-related facilities or welfare facilities for senior citizens among facilities for senior citizens
and children, and wholesale markets or retail markets among sales facilities;
2.  Detached  houses  (limited  to  multi-user  houses  and  multi-unit  houses),  multi-family  housing,
midwifery  clinics  or  postpartum  care  centers  among  Class  1  neighborhood  living  facilities,  and
communal  living  facilities  among  Class  2  neighborhood  living  facilities.


< 2013. 3. 23., 2022. 4. 29.>

< 2013. 3. 23., 2022. 4. 29.>

Article 48: (Installation of Stairs, Corridors and Doorway)
(1) Under the main clause of Article 49 (2) of the Act, stairs and corridors to be installed in a building with
a total floor area of not less than 200 square meters shall be installed in compliance with the standards
prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013; Apr. 29,
2022>
(2)  Under  the  main  clause  of  Article  49  (2)  of  the  Act,  doorways  of  a  building  falling  under  any
subparagraph  of  Article  39  (1)  shall  be  installed  in  compliance  with  the  standards  prescribed  by
Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013; Apr. 29, 2022>

Article 50: (Installation of Ceiling of Living Room)

Under the main clause of Article 49 (2) of the Act, the ceiling (referring to beams or the bottom side of the
floor board of the immediate upper floor and others similar thereto where no ceiling exists) of a living
room of a building used for purposes, other than factories, warehouse facilities, storage and treatment
facilities for hazardous substances, animal and plant-related facilities, resource recycling facilities, or
graveyard-related facilities, shall be installed in compliance with the standards prescribed by Ministerial
Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013; Mar. 24, 2014; Apr. 29, 2022>


< 2013. 3. 23., 2022. 4. 29.>

< 2015. 9. 22., 2017. 2. 3., 2019. 10. 22., 2020. 10. 8., 2022. 4. 29.>

< 2019. 10. 22.>


Article 51: (Daylighting of Living Room)
(1) Pursuant to the main clause of Article 49 (2) of the Act, the living rooms of detached houses and multi-
family housing, classrooms of schools among education and research facilities, inpatient rooms of medical
facilities, or guest rooms of lodging facilities shall be installed with windows, etc. or equipment for
daylighting and ventilation in compliance with the standards prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land,
Infrastructure and Transport. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013; Apr. 29, 2022>
(2) A living room (excluding a living room of a refuge floor) of each of the following buildings shall be
equipped with smoke exhaust systems pursuant to the main clause of Article 49 (2) of the Act: <Amended
on Sep. 22, 2015; Feb. 3, 2017; Oct. 22, 2019; Oct. 8, 2020; Apr. 29, 2022>
1. Buildings of at least six floors each, which are used for the following uses:
(a) Performance halls, religious assembly facilities, Internet computer game facilities, or communal
living facilities (applicable only where the total floor area used for the performance halls, religious
assembly facilities, or Internet computer game facilities is at least 300 square meters, respectively)
among Class 2 neighborhood living facilities;
(b) Cultural and assembly facilities;
(c) Religious facilities;
(d) Sales facilities;
(e) Transportation facilities;
(f) Medical facilities (excluding convalescent hospitals, and psychiatric hospitals);
(g) Research institutes among education and research facilities;
(h) Children-related facilities and welfare facilities for senior citizens among facilities for senior
citizens and children (excluding sanatoriums for senior citizens);
(i) Youth hostels among training facilities;
(j) Sports facilities;
(k) Business facilities;
(l) Lodging facilities;
(m) Amusement facilities;
(n) Tourist resting facilities;
(o) Funeral facilities;

2. Buildings used for the following uses:
(a) Convalescent hospitals or psychiatric hospitals among medical facilities;
(b) Sanatoriums for senior citizens, residential homes for persons with disabilities, and medical
rehabilitation facilities for persons with disabilities among facilities for senior citizens and children.
(c) Postnatal care centers among Class 1 neighborhood living facilities;
(3) Where an operable window is installed not more than 1.2 meters above the surface of the living room
in an officetel pursuant to the main clause of Article 49 (2) of the Act, a safety facility designed to prevent
falling accidents shall be installed in compliance with the standards prescribed by Ministerial Decree of
Land, Infrastructure and Transport. <Added on Jul. 16, 2009; Mar. 23, 2013; Apr. 29, 2022>
(4) Pursuant to Article 49 (3) of the Act, 11 or fewer stories of a building shall be equipped with a window
through which a firefighter can enter and a mark visible from the outside day and night. Provided, That
any of the following apartment buildings shall be excluded herefrom: <Amended on Oct. 22, 2019>
1. Apartment buildings with a refuge area, etc. under Article 46 (4) and (5);
2.  Apartment  buildings  with  an  emergency  elevator  installed  pursuant  to  Article  15  (2)  of  the
Regulations  on  Standards  for  Housing  Construction.


< 2013. 3. 23., 2022. 4. 29.>


Article 52: (Moisture-Proofing of Living Rooms)
Pursuant to the main clause of Article 49 (2) of the Act, the floors of living rooms, bathrooms or kitchens
falling under the following subparagraphs shall be protected against moisture according to the standards
prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport: <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013; Apr. 29,
2022>
1. Living rooms on the lowermost floor of a building (limited to cases where the floor is made of
wood);
2. Bathrooms of public baths, and kitchens of resting restaurants and confectioneries among Class 1
neighborhood living facilities;
3. Kitchens of general restaurants, resting restaurants and confectioneries, and bathrooms of lodging
facilities among Class 2 neighborhood living facilities.
