Article 53: (Installation of Partition Walls)
(1) Partition walls shall be installed in any of the following buildings in compliance with the standards
prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, pursuant to Article 49 (4) of the
Act: <Amended on Aug. 17, 2010; Mar. 23, 2013; Mar. 24, 2014; Nov. 28, 2014; Sep. 22, 2015; Oct. 22, 2019; Oct.
8, 2020>
1. Partition walls (excluding balconies not used for a living room or bedroom pursuant to the latter part
of subparagraph 14 of Article 2) between the units of multi-unit houses among detached houses, or
between dwelling units in multi-family housing (excluding dormitories);
2. Partition walls between bedrooms of a dormitory among multi-family housing, between inpatient
rooms of medical facilities, between classrooms of schools among education and research facilities, or
between guest rooms of lodging facilities;

3. Any of the following partition walls of a postnatal care center among Class 1 neighborhood living
facilities:
(a) Partition walls between rooms of nursing mothers;
(b) Partition walls between rooms of newborn babies;
(c) Partition walls between rooms of nursing mothers and newborn babies;
4. Partition walls between rooms of communal living facilities among Class 2 neighborhood living
facilities;
5. Partition walls between dwelling units of a welfare house for senior citizens under Article 32 (1) 3 of
the Act on the Welfare of the Senior Citizens (hereinafter referred to as “welfare house for senior
citizens”), among facilities for senior citizens or children;
6. Partition walls between rooms of a sanatorium for senior citizens among facilities for senior citizens
and children.
(2) The floor (excluding the floor of a toilet) of any of the following buildings shall be installed in
compliance with the standards prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport,
pursuant to Article 49 (4) of the Act: <Added on Nov. 28, 2014; Aug. 11, 2016; Oct. 22, 2019>
1. Multi-unit houses among detached houses;
2. Multi-family housing (excluding houses subject to approval of the housing construction project plan
under Article 15 of the Housing Act);
3. Officetels among business facilities;
4. Communal living facilities, among Class 2 neighborhood living facilities;
5. Communal living facilities among lodging facilities.

23.>

Article 54: (Chimneys Installed in Buildings)
Chimneys of a building shall be installed in conformity to the standards prescribed by Ministerial Decree
of Land, Infrastructure and Transport. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>



Article 55: (Screening Facility of Windows)
In cases where windows, etc. are installed within two meters from the borderline of the adjacent site in a
beeline, through which the interior of a neighboring house is seen, screening facilities shall be installed.

2019. 10. 22.>

Article 56: (Fire-Resistant Structures of Buildings)
(1) Main structural members and roofs of any of the following buildings (limited to underground floors in
cases of a building not exceeding two floors and falling under subparagraph 5) shall be of a fire-resistant
structure pursuant to the main clause of Article 50 (1) of the Act: Provided, That the same shall not apply
to one-storied accessory buildings with a total floor area not exceeding 50 square meters which have
fireproof exterior walls and fireproof bottom part of the eaves, and stage floors: <Amended on Jun. 30, 2009;

Feb. 18, 2010; Aug. 17, 2010; Mar. 23, 2013; Mar. 24, 2014; Feb. 3, 2017; Aug. 6, 2019; Oct. 22, 2019; Jan. 5,
2021>
1. A building used for performance halls or religious assembly facilities (applicable only where the total
floor area used for the relevant purpose is at least 300 square meters, respectively) among Class 2
neighborhood  living  facilities,  cultural  and  assembly  facilities  (excluding  exhibition  halls,  and
zoological and botanical gardens), religious facilities, or bar business among amusement facilities or
funeral facilities, in which the total floor area of auditorium or assembly rooms exceeds 200 square
meters (in cases of an outdoor auditorium, 1,000 square meters);
2. A building used for exhibition halls or zoological and botanical gardens among cultural and assembly
facilities, sales facilities, transportation facilities, gymnasiums or auditoriums established in education
and research facilities or training facilities, gymnasiums and playgrounds among sports facilities,
amusement facilities (excluding those used for bar business), warehouse facilities, storage and treatment
facilities for hazardous substances, motor vehicle-related facilities, broadcasting stations, telegraph and
telephone stations and movie studios among broadcasting and communication facilities, facilities for
cremation and for animal cremation among graveyard-related facilities, or tourist resting facilities, in
which the total floor area used for such purpose exceeds 500 square meters;
3. A building used for a factory in which the total floor area used for such purpose exceeds 2,000 square
meters: Provided, That factories with low fire hazards and prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land,
Infrastructure and Transport shall be excluded;
4. A building, the second floor of which is used for a multi-user house or multi-unit house among
detached houses, multi-family housing, Class 1 neighborhood living facilities (limited to facilities used
for medical purposes), communal living facilities among Class 2 neighborhood living facilities, medical
facilities, children-related facilities and welfare facilities for senior citizens among facilities for senior
citizens and children, youth hostels among training facilities, officetels among business facilities,
lodging facilities or funeral facilities, and in which the total floor area used for such purpose exceeds
400 square meters;
5. A building with at least three floors and underground floors: Provided, That buildings used for
detached houses (excluding multi-user houses and multi-unit houses), animal and plant-related facilities,
power  generating  facilities  (excluding  facilities  used  for  subsidiary  uses  of  the  power  plant),
correctional facilities and juvenile detention center, or graveyard-related facilities (excluding facilities
for cremation and for animal cremation) and any extension of not exceeding a gross area of 50 square
meters used for a control room among factories related to the steel industry shall be excluded.
(2) In cases of a building with a membrane structure, a fire-resistant structure may be required only for its
main structural members under the proviso of Article 50 (1) of the Act. <Amended on Oct. 22, 2019>


< 2013. 3.
23.>

< 2013. 3. 23.>

Article 57: (Firewalls of Large Building)
(1) A building with a total floor area of 1,000 or more square meters shall be divided by firewalls under
Article 50: (2) of the Act on the condition that the total floor area of partitions shall be less than 1,000
square meters: Provided, That the same shall not apply to the buildings of which main structural members
have a fire-resistant structure or are made of noncombustible materials, buildings falling under the proviso
of Article 56 (1) 5, or warehouse facilities which cannot be divided by firewalls due to the structure of
internal facilities.
(2) Matters necessary for the structure of firewalls under paragraph (1) shall be prescribed by Ministerial
Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>
(3) A wooden building with a total floor area of not less than 1,000 square meters shall be built of a
fireproof  structure  or  noncombustible  materials,  as  prescribed  by  Ministerial  Decree  of  Land,
Infrastructure  and  Transport.  <Amended  on  Mar.  23,  2013>



Article 58: (Buildings in Fire Prevention Zones)
Buildings of which main structural members and exterior walls need not be made of a fire-resistant
structure under Article 51 (1) of the Act shall be as follows:
1. One-storied accessory buildings with a total floor area of less than 30 square meters, the exterior
walls and underside of the eave of which have a fire-resistant structure or non-combustible materials;
2. Buildings which are used for wholesale markets and of which main structural members are made of
non-combustible materials.

Article 61-3: (Inspection on Violations regarding Manufacture and Distribution of Building Materials
and Measures Therefor)
(1) Where any violation is identified through an inspection conducted under Article 52-3 (2) of the Act,
the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, a Mayor/Do Governor, or the head of a Si/Gun/Gu
shall notify the construction participants, manufacturer, and distributor of the violation pursuant to
paragraph  (3)  of  that  Act,  and  may  take  the  following  measures  against  the  relevant  construction
participants,  manufacturer,  and  distributor:  <Amended  on  Jan.  20,  2017;  Oct.  22,  2019>
1. Measures to be taken against the construction participants:
(a) Where any part has been constructed using the relevant building material: Issuing an order to
correct the constructed portion, to suspend construction works of the relevant construction stage, and
to suspend the use of the relevant building material;
(b) Where the relevant building material is brought in, and kept at, the construction site: Issuing an
order to suspend the use of the relevant building material;
2. Measures to be taken against the manufacturer and the distributor: Requesting the head of the related
administrative agency to suspend the business of such manufacturer and distributor in accordance with
the related statutes.

(2) Upon receipt of a notice of the violation under paragraph (1) or an order issued under subparagraph 1
of that paragraph, the construction participants, manufacturer, and distributor shall prepare and submit an
action plan to the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, a Mayor/Do Governor, or the head of a
Si/Gun/Gu within seven days from the date of the receipt of such notice or order.
(3) Where the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, a Mayor/Do Governor, or the head of a
Si/Gun/Gu deems that corrective measures have been taken in accordance with the action plan submitted
under paragraph (2) (limited to the action plan prepared under an order issued under paragraph (1) 1 (a)),
he or she shall cancel the order for suspension of construction works.
[Moved from Article 18-3; Previous Article 61-3 moved to Article 63-2 <Oct. 22, 2019>]

Article 62: (Quality Control of Building Materials)
(1) "Composite materials (referring to materials consisting of noncombustible double-sided steel plates,
stone, concrete or materials similar thereto and combustible core materials), fire doors, or any other
building materials prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 52-4 (1) of the Act means any of the
following building materials: <Amended on Oct. 22, 2019; Oct. 8, 2020>
1. Composite materials under Article 52-4 (1) of the Act;
2. Finishing materials used for the exterior walls of a building, which are insulation materials;
3. A fire door under Article 64 (1) 1 through 3;
4. Other fireproof-related building materials prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure
and Transport.
(2) A manufacturer of building materials referred to in Article 52-4 (1) of the Act shall submit a quality
control report (hereinafter referred to as "quality control report") to a distributor of building materials
referred to in that paragraph; and the distributor shall deliver the quality control report to the project

contractor after verifying whether the building materials are in accord with the quality control report.
<Added on Oct. 22, 2019>
(3) Upon receipt of a quality control report under paragraph (2), the project contractor shall verify whether
the building materials are in accord with the quality control report; and shall submit all quality control
reports on materials used in the relevant building to the project supervisor. <Amended on Oct. 22, 2019>
(4) A project supervisor shall submit quality control reports submitted under paragraph (3) to the client as
prescribed in Article 25 (6) of the Act, accompanied by the report on the completion of construction
supervision, and the client shall submit them to the permitting authority when he or she applies for
approval for use of a building under Article 22 of the Act. <Amended on Oct. 22, 2019>
[Moved from Article 61-4 <Oct. 22, 2019>]

Article 63: (Institutions for Performance Testing of Building Materials)

Government-Funded Science and Technology Research Institutes" in Article 52-4 (2) of the Act means the

2. Persons whose ability to perform building-related quality tests meet the standards determined and

engineering business entities defined in the Construction Technology Promotion Act;
3. Testing and inspection agencies accredited pursuant to Article 23 of the Framework Act on National
Standards.


<2021. 12. 21.>]

Article 63-2: (Building Materials Subject to Quality Accreditation)
"Building materials and fire-resistant structures prescribed by Presidential Decree, such as fire doors and
composite materials" in Article 52-5 (1) of the Act means the following building materials and fire-
resistant structures (hereafter referred to as "building materials, etc." in Articles 63-4 and 63-5):
1. A composite material composed of steel plates and core materials prescribed by Ministerial Decree of
Land, Infrastructure and Transport, among composite materials referred to in Article 52-4 (1) of the
Act;
2. The following building materials and fire-resistant structures which are used for fire compartments in
a  building,  the  main  structural  member  of  which  has  a  fire-resistant  structure  or  are  made  of
noncombustible  materials:
(a) Automatic fire shutters;
(b) Fire-resistant filling structures, the performance of which is accredited, among building materials
prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport under Article 62 (1) 4;
3. Fire doors under each subparagraph of Article 64 (1);
4. Other building materials and fire-resistance structures prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land,
Infrastructure and Transport, the quality of which is required to be accredited for safety of buildings,
fire prevention, etc.
[Previous Article 63-2 moved to Article 63-6 <Dec. 21, 2021>]



Article 63-3: (Quality Accreditation Institute for Building Materials)
(1) "Institution prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 52-6 (1) of the Act means the Korea Institute
of Construction Technology.




Article 63-4: (Measures against Breach of Duty to Maintain Quality and Manage Building Materials)
(1) Where the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport receives notification under the former part of
Article 52-6: (5) of the Act, a manufacturer and distributor of quality-accredited materials, etc. referred to
in paragraph (3) of that Article (hereafter in this Article and Article 63-5) of the Act (hereafter in this
Article and Article 6355), " A business operator, etc. shall be notified of an illegal act and may take
measures classified as follows against a manufacturer, etc.:
1. Construction participants, etc. referred to in Article 25-2 (1) of the Act: Measures classified as
follows:
(a) Where quality-accredited materials, etc. are not used or there are parts that have not been
performed as accredited: An order to correct the constructed portion, suspend the construction works
of the relevant process, and suspend the use of building materials, etc. without quality accreditation.
(b) Where any building material, etc. without quality accreditation has been brought into or kept at a
construction site: An order to suspend the use of the relevant building material, etc.
2. Manufacturers and distributors: Requests to relevant institutions for suspension of business, etc.
under related statutes.
(2) Article 61-3 (2) and (3) shall apply mutatis mutandis to measures taken by the Minister of Land,
Infrastructure  and  Transport  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1).  In  such  cases,  "construction  participants,
manufacturers, and distributors" shall be construed as "manufacturers, etc." and "Minister of Land,
Infrastructure and Transport, a Mayor/Do Governor, and the head of a Si/Gun/Gu" as "Minister of Land,

Infrastructure and Transport."



Article 63-5: (Request for Data to Manufacturers)
The Korea Institute of Civil Engineering and Building Technology, which has been designated as an
institute for quality accreditation for building materials, etc. pursuant to Article 52-6 (1) of the Act and
Article 63-3: of this Decree, may request manufacturers, etc. to submit the following data pursuant to
Article 52-6: (6) of the Act:
1. Records of production and sale of building materials, etc. and quality-accredited materials, etc.;
2. Performance record of using building materials, etc. and quality-accredited materials, etc. by
construction site;
3. Quality control manual;
4. Other data determined and publicly notified by the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport,
which can verify the appropriateness of quality management of quality-accredited materials, etc., such
as records relating to manufacturing processes.

<2021. 12. 21.>]

Article 63-6: (Anti-Crime for Buildings)
“Buildings prescribed by Presidential Decree” in Article 53-2 (2) of the Act means any of the following:
<Amended on Dec. 31, 2018>
1. Multi-unit houses, apartment houses, tenement houses, and multi-household houses;
2. Retail shops selling daily necessities, among Class 1 neighborhood living facilities;
3. Communal living facilities among Class 2 neighborhood living facilities;
4. Cultural and assembly facilities (excluding zoological and botanical gardens);
5. Education and research facilities (excluding research institutions and libraries);
6. Facilities for senior citizens or children;
7. Training facilities;
8. Officetels, among business facilities;
9. Communal living facilities, among lodging facilities.
[Moved from Article 63-2 <Dec. 21, 2021>]



Article 64: (Classification of Fire Door)
(1) Fire doors shall be classified as follows:
1. FD60+ fire doors: Fire doors that can withstand exposure to smoke and flames for at least 60 minutes
and heat for at least 30 minutes;
2. FD60 fire doors: Fire doors that can withstand exposure to smoke and flames for at least 60 minutes;
3. FD 30 fire doors: Fire doors that can withstand exposure to smoke and flames for at least 30 minutes,
but less than 60 minutes.
(2) Standards for recognition of fire doors under the subparagraphs of paragraph (1) shall be prescribed by
Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport.

Article 77: (Cases of Building Sites Extending Over Areas, Districts or Zones)
Where a site extends over an area, district or zone under Article 54 (1) of the Act, a person who intends to
have the provisions pertaining to the buildings, sites, etc. in the area, district or zone to which a majority
of the site concerned belongs applied to the entire site concerned shall submit (including submission by
means of electronic documents) to the permitting authority the area of the site concerned under the
categories of areas, districts or zones and matters concerning the area, district or zone he or she intends to
have the aforementioned provisions applied to the entire site concerned.

Article 81: (Construction of Party Walls and Connecting Corridors)
(1) "Area prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 59 (1) 1 of the Act, means any of the following
areas: <Amended on Oct. 29, 2008; Dec. 12, 2012; Oct. 14, 2014; Sep. 22, 2015>
1. A commercial area (in cases of public-use buildings or multi-family housing, limited to those fitted
with sprinklers or other similar automatic fire extinguishing systems);
2. A residential area (limited to where the building owner and the site owner has agreed on the
construction of party walls);
3. A zone determined by the permitting authority by a building ordinance for preserving and promoting
the cityscape and Hanoks;

4. A construction agreement zone.
(2) Deleted. <May 8, 2006>
(3) Party walls referred to in Article 59 (1) 1 of the Act, shall conform to the following standards:
<Amended on Oct. 29, 2008; Oct. 14, 2014>
1. The main structural members shall have a fire-resistant structure;
2. Finishing materials shall be noncombustible;
(4) Where party walls are erected in the areas (excluding construction agreement zones) referred to in
paragraph (1), matters necessary for the uses of buildings subject to party wall construction, number of
buildings built with party walls, number of floors of buildings built with party walls, etc. shall be
determined by a building ordinance.  <Amended  on  Oct.  29,  2008;  Oct.  14,  2014>
(5) "Standards prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 59 (1) 2 of the Act, means the following:
<Amended on Oct. 29, 2008; Aug. 6, 2019>
1. The main structural members shall have a fire-resistant structure;
2. Finishing materials shall be noncombustible;
3. Windows of a size equivalent to at least 1/10 of the wall area shall be installed in an enclosed
structure:  Provided,  That  this  shall  not  apply  where  ventilation  facilities  are  installed  on  the
underground  floor;
4. Neither the width nor height shall exceed five meters, respectively: Provided, That if the permitting
authority deems it necessary for ensuring smooth passage, considering the use, scale, etc. of the
building, the standards may be applied leniently following deliberation by a local building committee;
5. Automatic fire shutters or fire doors shall be installed in parts connecting a building to its corridor or
passage;
6. The total area of the site where a connecting corridor is installed, shall not exceed the maximum scale
of development activities conducted under Article 55 of the Enforcement Decree of the National Land
Planning and Utilization Act: Provided, That this shall not apply within district-unit planning zones.
(6) The safety of corridors or connecting passages referred to in Article 59 (1) 2 of the Act shall be
verified by a certified architect or a building structural engineer. <Amended on Oct. 29, 2008; Jul. 16, 2009;
May 17, 2016; Jul. 19, 2016>

Article 82: (Limits on Heights of Buildings)
(1)  The  permitting  authority  shall  consider  the  following  matters  when  designating  and  publicly
announcing the heights of buildings within a specific block pursuant to Article 60 (1) of the Act: <Amended
on Apr. 10, 2012; Oct. 14, 2014>
1. A land use plan, such as urban/Gun management planning;
2. Width of a road abutting the relevant block;
3. Capacity of arterial facilities, such as water supply and sewerage of the relevant block;
4. An urban scenery and landscape plan;
5. A future development plan of the relevant city.
(2) To designate the heights of buildings within a specific block under paragraph (1), the permitting
authority shall submit the relevant case to the competent local building committee for deliberation. In such
cases, procedures for hearing the opinions of residents shall be governed by Article 8 of the Framework
Act on the Regulation of Land Use. <Amended on Jun. 29, 2011; Oct. 14, 2014>
(3) The permitting authority may vary the heights of buildings in the same block according to the uses and
shapes of such buildings.
(4) Detailed standards for relaxing the limits on the heights of buildings pursuant to the proviso of Article
60 (1) of the Act, shall be determined by a building ordinance, in consideration of the matters referred to
in the subparagraphs of paragraph (1). <Amended on Feb. 18, 2010; Oct. 14, 2014>

Article 86: (Limits on Heights of Buildings for Solar Access)
(1) Where a building is constructed in an exclusive residential area or a general residential area, each part
of  the  building  shall  be  constructed  by  maintaining  at  least  the  distance  determined  by  a  building
ordinance within the following applicable distance, due north from the boundary line of the adjoining site
under Article 61 (1) of the Act: <Amended on Jul. 6, 2015; Sep. 12, 2023>
1. Parts not exceeding 10 meters tall: At least 1.5 meters from the boundary line of the adjoining site;
2. Parts exceeding 10 meters tall: At least 1/2 of the height of each part of the building from the
boundary line of the adjoining site.
(2) Paragraph (1) shall not apply to any of the following cases: <Added on Jul. 6, 2015; May 17, 2016; Jul. 19,
2016; Dec. 29, 2017>
1. Where buildings are constructed on both sites in any of the following zones, and the sites abut on a
road, which is at least 20 meters wide (including a road for the exclusive use of motor vehicles,
pedestrians, or bicycles; and where the road abuts on any public open space, a green belt, a plaza, or any
other urban or Gun planning facility which does not degrade the aesthetics of the buildings, including
such facilities):
(a) A district-unit planning zone designated under Article 51 of the National Land Planning and
Utilization Act, a scenic district referred to in Article 37 (1) 1 of that Act;
(b) A focused landscape management area referred to in Article 9 (1) 4 of the Landscape Act;
(c) A special street zone designated under Article 77-2 (1) of the Act;
(d) Other zones designated and publicly announced by the permitting authority to improve the
cityscape;
2. Where buildings are constructed on both sites within a construction agreement zone (applicable only
to where a construction agreement concluded under Article 77-4 (1) of the Act stipulates that buildings
shall be constructed a specific distance apart);
3. Where the adjoining site due north of the site on which buildings stand belongs to a specific-use area,
other than an exclusive residential area or a general residential area.
(3) Multi-family housing shall satisfy the following criteria pursuant to Article 61 (2) of the Act: Provided,
That subparagraph 1 shall not apply to any multi-household house with a horizontal distance determined
by a building ordinance, within at least one meter perpendicularly from the wall on which windows, etc.
for daylighting are installed, to the boundary of the adjoining site: <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; May 31, 2013;
Jul. 6, 2015; Nov. 2, 2021>
1. The height of each part of a building (excluding dormitories) shall not exceed two times (four times
in cases of a building within a neighboring commercial area or semi-residential area) the distance
perpendicularly from the wall of the relevant part, on which windows, etc. for daylighting are installed,
to the boundary of the adjoining site;

2. Where at least two buildings stand on the same site, facing each other (including where respective
parts of one building face one another), at least the following distances shall be maintained between the
respective parts of the buildings: Provided, That such distances shall allow all dwelling units in the site
to have solar access for at least two consecutive hours during the period from 9 a.m. to 3 p.m. on the
day of the winter solstice:
(a) At least the distance determined by a building ordinance within at least 0.5 times (0.25 times in
cases of urban-type residential housing) the height of each part of buildings perpendicularly from the
wall on which windows, etc. for daylighting are installed;
(b) Notwithstanding item (a), where among buildings facing each other, the main opening (referring
to the opening of the part where the living room and main bedroom are located) of the higher
building (limited to where the direction of the axis of two buildings facing each other, is between due
east and due west in a clockwise direction centered at the higher building) faces the lower building, at
least the distance determined by a building ordinance, or at least 10 meters, within at least 0.5 times
(0.25 times in cases of urban-type residential housing) the height of each part of the lower building
and within at least 10 meters;
(c) Notwithstanding item (a), where a building faces its incidental facilities or welfare facilities, at
least one times the height of each part in such incidental facilities or welfare facilities;
(d) Where the surface of a wall without a daylight window (referring to windows at least 0.5 square
meters wide) and a side wall face each other, at least eight meters;
(e) Where a side wall faces another side wall (including where a balcony (including openings for
entry) with a floor area of not more than three square meters and without a window for daylighting is
installed on one of the side walls facing each other), at least four meters;
3. Subparagraph 2 (a) through (c) shall not apply where at least two buildings face each other across a
road as defined in Article 2 (1) 11 of the Act in a housing complex referred to in Article 3 (1) 4, on
condition that subparagraph 1 applies to such cases, deeming the centerline of the relevant road to be
the boundary of the adjoining site.
(4) "Height prescribed by Presidential Decree" in the provisions, with the exception of the subparagraphs,
of Article 61 (3) of the Act means the height determined and publicly notified by the Special Self-
Governing City Mayor, the Special Self-Governing Province Governor, or the head of a Si/Gun/Gu within
the height limits referred to in paragraph (1). <Amended on Oct. 14, 2014; Jul. 6, 2015>
(5) The Special Self-Governing City Mayor, the Special Self-Governing Province Governor, or the head
of a Si/Gun/Gu shall hear the opinions of relevant residents, as prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land,
Infrastructure and Transport before he or she publicly notifies the heights of buildings under paragraph
(4): Provided, That this shall not apply to areas provided in any of Article 61 (3) 1 through 6 of the Act,
which have deliberated upon by the building committee. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013; Oct. 14, 2014; May 17,
2016>

(6) For purposes of paragraphs (1) through (5), if any of the following facilities or sites exists between a
site on which a building is to be constructed and another site, the boundary of the site on the opposite side
(in cases of multi-family housing, the centerline of the boundary of the adjoining site and the boundary of
the site on the opposite side) shall be deemed the boundary of the adjoining site: <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009;
Nov. 11, 2014; Jul. 6, 2015; May 17, 2016; Nov. 2, 2021>
1. A park (excluding any park determined by the permitting authority, after deliberation by the local
building committee, to have solar access, among urban parks as defined in subparagraph 3 of Article 2
of Act on Urban Parks and Green Areas), a road, a railway, a river, a plaza, a public open area, a green
belt, a retarding basin, a road for the exclusive use of motor vehicles, and an amusement park;
2. The following sites (limited to those where no building exists):
(a) A site up to two meters wide (referring to the shortest distance from the boundary line of the site);
(b) A site not exceeding the limits on partition of sites provided in the subparagraphs of Article 80;
3. An open area in which construction is prohibited, other than a site referred to in subparagraph 1 or 2.
(7) For purposes of paragraphs (1) through (5), if any facility or site specified in the subparagraphs of
paragraph (6) exists on a site where a building (limited to multi-family housing) is to be constructed, the
centerline of the boundary of the relevant site facing such facility or site specified in the subparagraphs of
paragraph (6) may be determined as the boundary of the adjoining site, subject to deliberation by the local
building committee. <Added on Sep. 4, 2018>

Article 87: (Principles of Installation of Building Service)
(1) Building service shall be installed not to hinder the safety, fire prevention, hygiene, and rational use of
energy,  information  and  communications  of  a  building,  and  to  facilitate  easy  maintenance  and
management of building service by making the cross-sectional area and access holes for repairing piping
pits and ducts to ensure ready maintenance and repair of the relevant equipment.
(2) Technical standards applicable to building service, such as water supply, drainage, cooling, heating,
ventilation, and lightning arresters installed in a building, shall be prescribed by Ministerial Decree of
Land, Infrastructure and Transport, and the technical standards for building service related to rational
energy use shall be determined upon consultation with the Minister of Trade, Industry and Energy.
<Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>
(3) Facilities and equipment to be installed in every building for persons with disabilities shall comply
with detailed standard designs of amenities prepared and distributed under Article 14 of the Act on
Guarantee of Convenience Promotion of Persons with Disabilities, Older Persons, and Pregnant Women
and Nursing Mothers <Amended on Dec. 12, 2012>
(4) A master antenna, cable broadcasting reception equipment, satellite broadcasting reception equipment,
FM radio reception equipment, or joint reception equipment for media broadcasts may be installed in
buildings for the smooth reception of media broadcasts: Provided, That the joint reception equipment for
media broadcasts shall be installed in the following buildings: <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; Dec. 12, 2012>

1. Multi-family housing;
2. A building with a total floor area of at least 5,000 square meters, used for a business facility or
lodging facility.
(5) Standards for the installation of the broadcasting reception equipment referred to in paragraph (4) shall
be determined and publicly notified by the Minister of Science and ICT. <Added on Jul. 16, 2009; Mar. 23,
2013; Jul. 26, 2017>
(6) An area available for installing electric equipment necessary for supplying electric power by an electric
utility business operator as defined in subparagraph 2 of Article 2 of the Electric Utility Act shall be
secured in the site of a building with a total floor area of at least 500 square meters, as prescribed by
Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport. <Added on Jul. 16, 2009; Mar. 23, 2013>
(7) Each local government may prescribe the following matters by its ordinance to prevent damage from
sea breeze, salt, etc. such as early corrosion of materials and machinery equipment of a building, for an
area in which such damage is likely to occur: <Added on Feb. 18, 2010>
1. Design standards for durability against sea breeze, salt, etc.;
2. Allowance standards for durability against sea breeze, salt, etc.;
3. Other matters necessary to prevent damage from sea breeze, salt, etc.
(8) Mailboxes installed in buildings shall meet the standards referred to in Article 37-2 of the Postal
Service Act. <Added on Oct. 14, 2014>

<1995. 12. 30.>

Article 88: Deleted. <Dec. 30, 1995>



Article 89: (Installation of Passenger Elevators)
"Buildings prescribed by Presidential Decree" in the former part of Article 64 (1) of the Act means
buildings with six floors where one or more direct staircases are installed for every floor area of 300 or
fewer square meters of living rooms on each floor.


< 2013. 3. 23.>

Article 90: (Installation of Emergency Elevators)
(1) Emergency elevators (including the platform and shaft of an emergency elevator; hereafter in this
Article the same shall apply) shall, under Article 64 (2) of the Act, be installed in buildings of which
height exceeds 31 meters in not less than the number according to the criteria in each of the following
subparagraphs: Provided, That this shall not apply to cases an elevator installed under Article 64 (1) of the
Act is of the structure of an emergency elevator:
1. Buildings of which height exceeds 31 meters and of which largest floor area among the floor areas of
each floor is not more than 1,500 square meters: Not less than one unit;
2. Buildings of which height exceeds 31 meters and of which largest floor area among the floor areas of
each floor exceeds 1,500 square meters: One unit plus one unit for every not more than 3,000 square
meters in excess of 1,500 square meters.
(2) When installing two or more emergency elevators under paragraph (1), they shall be installed at
specific intervals not to impede firefighting at the time of a fire.
(3)  Matters  necessary  for  the  structure,  etc.  of  emergency  elevators  installed  in  buildings  shall  be
prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>




Article 91: (Installation of Evacuation Elevators)
An evacuation elevator referred to in Article 64 (3) of the Act (including the platform and shaft of an
evacuation elevator; hereafter in this Article the same shall apply) shall be installed in conformity to each
of the following standards:
1. The floor area of the platform of each elevator shall be at least six square meters;
2. A shaft connecting each floor to the refuge floor shall be installed in a single structure;
3. Lighting equipment that operates on a backup power source shall be installed;
4. A sign stating that the relevant elevator is an evacuation elevator shall be installed at a prominent
place near the entrance to the elevator;
5. The elevator shall meet other standards for the structure, equipment, etc. prescribed by Ministerial
Decree of Ministry of Land, Infrastructure and Transport to prevent fire and reduce damage.

<2013. 2. 20.>

Article 91-3: (Cooperation with Relevant Specialized Engineers)
(1) The designer of any of the following buildings shall seek cooperation from a building structural
engineer in verifying the structural safety of the relevant building pursuant to Article 32 (1): <Amended on
Jul. 16, 2009; Mar. 23, 2013; May 31, 2013; Nov. 28, 2014; Sep. 22, 2015; Dec. 4, 2018>
1. A building with at least six floors;
2. A building of unique structures;
3. A public-use building;
4. A quasi-public-use building;
5. A piloti-type building with at least three floors;
6. A building prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, among buildings
referred to in Article 32 (2) 6.
(2) Each person who installs building service in a building with a total floor area of at least 10,000 square
meters (excluding warehouse facilities) or in a building prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land,

Infrastructure and Transport which consumes a large amount of energy, shall seek cooperation from the
relevant specialized engineers, as prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport,
according to the following classification: <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; Mar. 23, 2013; May 17, 2016; May 2,
2017>
1. Electricity, elevators (limited to electricity), and lightning rods: Professional engineers in building
electric equipment or professional engineers in electric power generation, transmission, and distribution,
registered under the Professional Engineers Act;
2. Facilities for water supply, water distribution, drainage, ventilation, heating, fire extinguishing, and
smoke exhaust, filth-treating equipment, and elevators (limited to machinery): Professional engineers in
building mechanical facilities or professional engineers in air-conditioning and refrigerating machinery,
registered under the Professional Engineers Act;
3. Gas facilities: Professional engineers in building mechanical facilities, professional engineers in air-
conditioning  and  refrigerating  machinery,  or  professional  gas  engineers,  registered  under  the
Professional  Engineers  Act.
(3) The designer and the project supervisor of a building which requires land excavation works in a depth
of at least 10 meters or construction of retaining walls, etc. at least five meters tall, shall seek cooperation
from professional engineers in the field of civil engineering, or professional geological or geotechnical
engineers in the field of national land development registered under the Professional Engineers Act about
the land excavation works, etc. as prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport.
<Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; Dec. 13, 2010; Mar. 23, 2013; May 17, 2016>
(4) Every designer and project supervisor shall seek cooperation from the relevant specialized engineers,
where deemed necessary for safety reasons, where required by relevant statutes or regulations, or where
requested by the client pursuant to the contract for design service or supervision contract.
(5)  Every  project  supervisor  of  a  building  of  unique  structures  or  a  high-rise  building  shall  seek
cooperation from a building structural engineer whenever the building reaches the construction stages
provided for in each item of Article 19 (3) 1 and 2. <Amended on Nov. 28, 2014; May 17, 2016>
(6) When supervising construction works for the structural safety of a building under Article 48 of the Act,
a project supervisor of a piloti-type building with at least three floors shall obtain cooperation from a
related specialized engineer specified in Article 67 (1) 1 through 3 of the Act whenever the construction
works reach the stage specified in Article 18-2 (2) 3 (b). In such cases, the related specialized engineer
may have an engineer under his or her jurisdiction, qualified as a special-grade or high-quality engineer
specified  in  subparagraph  3  (d)  (i)  of  Appendix  1  of  the  Enforcement  Decree  of  the  Construction
Technology  Promotion  Act,  supervise  the  construction  works.  <Added  on  Dec.  4,  2018>
(7)  Every  relevant  specialized  engineer  who  has  cooperated  with  a  certified  architect  or  a  project
supervisor under paragraphs (1) through (6), shall verify the construction site and affix his or her name
and seal to the design documents, or progress supervision report and final supervision report prepared
thereby, together with the designer or project supervisor. <Amended on Jul. 16, 2009; May 31, 2013; Nov. 28,

2014; Dec. 4, 2018>
(8) Every building structural engineer who has cooperated with a designer in verifying structural safety
under Article 32 (1), shall affix his or her name and seal to the structure-related documents, including the
structural drawing of the building, together with the designer after verifying structural safety. <Added on
Jul. 16, 2009; May 31, 2013; Nov. 28, 2014; Dec. 4, 2018>
(9) "Period prescribed by Presidential Decree" in the provisions, with the exception of the subparagraphs,
of Article 67 (1) of the Act means two years. <Added on Jul. 19, 2016; Dec. 4, 2018>


< 2021. 8. 10.>


Article 91-4: (Technical Standards for Building Service Recognized as New Technology or New
Products)
(1) A person who intends to obtain recognition of technical standards under Article 68 (4) of the Act shall
submit documents prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport to the Minister
of Land, Infrastructure and Transport.
(2) In receipt of documents submitted under paragraph (1), the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and
Transport may request the Korea Institute of Civil Engineering and Building Technology to examine
whether the relevant technology or product is new, advanced, and applicable to the field. <Amended on Aug.
10, 2021>
(3) Where the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport deems that a technology and product for
which a request for recognition of technical standards is filed under paragraph (1) is new, advanced, and
applicable to the field, he or she may recognize such technical standards subject to deliberation by the
Central Building Committee.

(4) In recognizing technical standards pursuant to paragraph (3), the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and
Transport may determine the effective period, which shall be for any term not exceeding five years. In
such  cases,  the  effective  period  may  be  extended,  as  prescribed  by  Ministerial  Decree  of  Land,
Infrastructure  and  Transport.
(5) Where the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport recognizes the technical standards under
paragraphs (3) and (4), he or she shall publicly notify the standards and effective period in the Official
Gazette; and shall post them on the website.
(6) Except as provided in paragraphs (1) through (5), further details necessary for evaluating building
service technology and products under Article 68 (4) of the Act and recognition of technical standards
therefor may be determined and publicly notified by the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport.



Article 92: (Administration of Construction Monitoring)
(1) "Period prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 68-3 (1) of the Act means three years.
(2) The Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport may designate an entity that has the following
human resources and organization as a specialized institution to conduct construction monitoring under
Article 68-3: (2) of the Act:
1.  Human  resources:  At  least  five  persons  who  have  qualifications  for  engineers  in  the  field  of
construction  under  the  National  Technical  Qualifications  Act;
2. Organization: An exclusive organization capable of conducting construction monitoring.

Article 105: (Designation of Special Building Zones)
(1) "Project zone prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 69 (1) 1 (b) of the Act, means any of the
following: <Amended on Apr. 21, 2009; Jul. 30, 2009; Dec. 12, 2012; Apr. 29, 2014; Jul. 28, 2014; Oct. 14, 2014;
Dec. 28, 2015; Feb. 27, 2018>
1. Project zone for the Administrative City designated under the Special Act on the Construction of
Administrative City in Yeongi-Gongju Area for Follow-up Measures for New Administrative Capital;
2.  Project  zone  for  innovation  cities  designated  under  the  Special  Act  on  the  Construction  and
Development  of  Innovation  Cities;
3. Free economic zone designated under Article 4 of the Special Act on Designation and Management
of Free Economic Zones;
4.  Project  zone  for  housing  site  development  designated  under  the  Housing  Site  Development
Promotion  Act;
5. Public housing zone as defined in subparagraph 2 of Article 2 of the Special Act on Public Housing;
6. Deleted; <Oct. 14, 2014>
7. Urban development zone designated under the Urban Development Act;
8. Deleted; <Oct. 14, 2014>
9. Deleted; <Oct. 14, 2014>
10. Project zone for constructing the National Center for Asian Culture under the Special Act on the
Development of Asian Cultural Hub City;
11. Special planning zone for creative development by means of design competition, etc. among
district-unit planning zones designated under Article 51 of the National Land Planning and Utilization
Act;

12. Deleted; <Oct. 14, 2014>
13. Deleted. <Oct. 14, 2014>
(2) "Project zone prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 69 (1) 2 (b) of the Act, means any of the
following: <Added on Oct. 14, 2014>
1. Free economic zone designated under Article 4 of the Special Act on Designation and Management
of Free Economic Zones;
2.  Project  zone  for  housing  site  development  designated  under  the  Housing  Site  Development
Promotion  Act;
3. Rearrangement zone designated under the Act on the Improvement of Urban Areas and Residential
Environments;
4. Urban development zone designated under the Urban Development Act;
5. Renewal promotion zone designated under the Special Act on the Promotion of Urban Renewal;
6. Project zone for a free international city designated under the Special Act on the Establishment of
Jeju Special Self-Governing Province and the Development of Free International City;
7. Special planning zone for creative development by means of design competition, etc. among district-
unit planning zones designated under Article 51 of the National Land Planning and Utilization Act;
8. Tourist attraction, tourism complex, or special tourist zone designated under Articles 52 and 70 of the
Tourism Promotion Act;
9. Cultural zone designated under Article 18 of the Regional Culture Promotion Act.
(3) “City or area prescribed by Presidential Decree” in Article 69 (1) 2 (c) of the Act, means any of the
following: <Amended on Dec. 13, 2010; Jun. 29, 2011; Mar. 23, 2013; Oct. 14, 2014>
1. Deleted. <Oct. 14, 2014>
2.  Area  where  buildings  or  spatial  environments  prescribed  by  Ministerial  Decree  of  Land,
Infrastructure  and  Transport  are  created  to  promote  an  architectural  culture;
2-2. Area that fully meets the following requirements, as it is necessary to promote the multiple use of
land combining various functions, such as residence, commerce, and business, therein:
(a) It shall be within an urban district;
(b) It shall be necessary to lift restrictions on construction within a specific use area designated under
Article 71: of the Enforcement Decree of the National Land Planning and Utilization Act;
3. Other cities or areas deemed necessary by a Mayor/Do Governor to be designated as a special
building zone to create a cityscape, and to improve construction technologies and construction-related
systems.

Article 107: (Procedures for Designation of Special Building Zones)
(1) The details of each urban/Gun management plan referred to in Article 71 (1) 4 of the Act shall be as
follows: <Amended on Apr. 10, 2012>

1. Matters concerning specific-use areas, specific-use districts, and specific-use zones designated under
Articles 36 through 38, 38-2, 39, and 40 of the National Land Planning and Utilization Act, and Articles
30 through 32 of the Enforcement Decree of that Act;
2. Matters concerning the status of urban/Gun planning facilities determined and installed in accordance
with the urban/Gun management plan prepared under Article 43 of the National Land Planning and
Utilization  Act,  and  matters  concerning  the  new  installment  and  change  of  urban/Gun  planning
facilities;
3. Matters concerning the designation of district-unit planning zones, details of district unit plans,
formulation and change of district unit plans, etc. under Articles 50 through 52 of the National Land
Planning and Utilization Act, and Articles 43 through 47 of the Enforcement Decree of that Act.
(2) "Matters prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 71 (1) 7 of the Act, means the following:
<Amended on Dec. 13, 2010; Apr. 10, 2012; Oct. 14, 2014>
1. Matters concerning urban/Gun planning facilities determined and installed in accordance with the
urban/Gun management plan under Article 43 of the National Land Planning and Utilization Act in
areas adjacent to special building zones;
2. Matters concerning the designation of district-unit planning zones in areas adjacent to special
building zones and details of such district unit planning;
2-2. Matters concerning the reflection of standards for architectural design under Article 21 of the
Framework Act on Building;
3. Where a private expert has been commissioned under Article 23 of the Framework Act on Building,
matters thereabout;
4. Matters concerning the multiple use of land under Article 105 (3) 2-2 (limited to applications for
designation of an area referred to in Article 105 (3) 2-2).
(3) Upon the designation of a special building zone or revision or cancellation of such designation
pursuant to Article 71 (7) of the Act, the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, or a Mayor/Do
Governor shall promptly publicly notify the following matters in the Official Gazette (in the public gazette
in cases of a Mayor/Do Governor): <Amended on Apr. 10, 2012; Mar. 23, 2013; Oct. 14, 2014; Jan. 8, 2021>
1. Purposes of such designation, revision, or cancellation;
2. Location, scope, and area of the special building zone;
3. Major details about the scale, use, etc. of buildings in the special building zone;
4. Matters concerning the method of placing orders, such as building design, construction supervision,
and execution of construction;
5. Matters concerning the new establishment of urban/Gun planning facilities, and the change thereof,
the formulation and amendment of district unit plans;
6. Other matters deemed necessary by the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, or the
Mayor/Do Governor.

(4) Where an applicant for designation of a special building zone intends to apply for revising such
designation  of  a  special  building  zone  under  Article  71  (9)  of  the  Act,  as  any  of  the  following  is
applicable, it shall file an application for revised designation with the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and
Transport, the competent Special Metropolitan City Mayor, Metropolitan City Mayor, or Do Governor
with materials prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport. In such cases,
Article 71: (4) and (5) of the Act shall apply mutatis mutandis to the revised designation of special building
zones: <Amended on Apr. 10, 2012; Mar. 23, 2013; Oct. 14, 2014; Jan. 8, 2021>
1. Where the area of a special building zone increases or decreases by at least 1/10 (1/20 where the area
of a special building zone is less than 100,000 square meters);
2. Where the matters concerning the urban/Gun management plan of a special building zone are revised;
3. Where the method of placing orders, such as building design, construction supervision, and execution
of construction, is revised;
4. Other cases prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport, such as revising
the purpose of designating the special building zone.
(5) Except as provided in paragraphs (1) through (4), further details necessary for designating special
building zones shall be determined and publicly notified by the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and
Transport. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>



Article 107-2: (Procedures for Recommending Designation of Special Building Zones)
(1) Any person who intends to propose the designation of a special building zone pursuant to Article 71
(2) of the Act may seek opinions from the head of a Si/Gun/Gu while presenting data listed in paragraph
(1) of that Article.
(2) Upon receipt of a request for his or her opinion pursuant to paragraph (1), the head of a Si/Gun/Gu
shall review the necessity to designate a special building zone, feasibility, public nature, etc. and any
matter regarding evacuation, disaster prevention, etc. and shall notify the relevant applicant of his or her
opinion. In such cases, a civilian expert commissioned by the head of a Si/Gun/Gu may be consulted on
under Article 23 of the Framework Act on Building.
(3) A person who intends to propose the designation of a special building zone pursuant to Article 71 (2)
of the Act shall obtain written consent from any of the following persons before proposing the designation
to the Mayor/Do Governor. In such cases, the method of written consent of the landowner shall be
prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport:
1. An owner of land corresponding to at least 2/3 of the area of land subject to entrustment (excluding
the area of State-owned or public land);
2. The property management authority of State-owned or public land (limited to cases where State-
owned or public land is included therein).
(4) A person who intends to propose the designation of a special building zone pursuant to Article 71 (2)
of the Act shall submit the following documents to the competent Mayor/Do Governor:
1. Data referred to in the subparagraphs of Article 71 (1) of the Act;
2. Opinions of the head of a Si/Gun/Gu pursuant to paragraph (2) (limited to where opinions are
requested);
3. Written consent of the landowner and the property management authority under paragraph (3).
(5) The Mayor/Do Governor shall determine whether to designate a special building zone after reviewing
the necessity, feasibility, public nature, etc. of the designation of the special building zone, matters
including evacuation and disaster prevention within 45 days from the date of receipt of the documents
under paragraph (4). In such cases, it shall be deliberated on by a building committee established by the
relevant Mayor/Do Governor after hearing opinions of the head of the competent Si/Gun/Gu (excluding

where a written opinion prescribed in paragraph (4) 2 is received).
(6) The Mayor/Do Governor shall notify the person who proposed the designation of a special building
zone of the results thereof within 14 days from the date he or she determines whether to grant the
designation under paragraph (5).
(7) Paragraphs (1) through (6) shall apply mutatis mutandis to a proposal for revised designation of a
special building zone designated pursuant to paragraph (5).
(8) Except as provided in paragraphs (1) through (7), details necessary for designating a special building
zone shall be determined and publicly notified by the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport.

Article 108: (Deliberation on Buildings in Special Building Zones)
(1) Cases subject to deliberation on revision by a local building committee under Article 72 (5) of the Act,
shall be as follows: <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>
1. Where permission for revision is required under Article 16 of the Act;
2. Where permission or notification is required to make a change under Article 19 (2) of the Act;

3. Where the exterior design, shape or color of a building is to be changed;
4. Where matters prescribed by Ministerial Decree of Land, Infrastructure and Transport among those
referred to in each subparagraph of Article 72 (1) of the Act are to be revised.
(2) Where a designer participates in the construction of a building under the former part of Article 72 (8)
of the Act, the contractor and the project supervisor shall reflect the advice of the designer, unless a
compelling reason not to do so exists.
(3) The duties of designers referred to in the latter part of Article 72 (8) of the Act are as follows:
1. Monitoring under Article 72 (6) of the Act;
2. Advice on design change;
3. Advice for realizing the design intent regarding the building design, cityscape, etc.;
4. Other duties entrusted by the ordering agency.
(4) The remuneration for the duties of designers prescribed in paragraph (3), shall be determined and
publicly  notified  by  the  Minister  of  Land,  Infrastructure  and  Transport  within  the  standards  for
compensation for engineering projects under Article 31 of the Engineering Industry Promotion Act.
<Amended on Jan. 17, 2011; Mar. 23, 2013>
(5) Except as provided in paragraphs (1) through (4), detailed matters concerning designers’ participation
in  the  construction  of  a  building  in  a  special  building  zone  after  deliberation  on  the  building  was
completed and the building permission thereof has been granted, shall be determined and publicly notified
by the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport. <Amended on Mar. 23, 2013>


< 2013. 6. 17.>

< 2017. 1. 26., 2022. 11. 29.>

Article 109: (Special Cases concerning Application of Relevant Statutes or Regulations)
(1) "Provisions prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 73 (1) 2 of the Act means Articles 10, 13, 29,
35, 37, 50, and 52 of the Regulations on Standards, etc. of Housing Construction. <Amended on Jun. 17,
2013>
(2) Where the permitting authority intends to leniently apply the standards or functions, etc. under Articles
12 and 13 of the Act on Installation and Management of Firefighting Systems under Article 73 (3) of the
Act, it shall undergo the deliberation by a local fire-fighting technology deliberation committee under
Article 30: (2) of the Fire-Fighting System Installation Business Act or consult the head of a fire defense
headquarter or the head of a fire station. <Amended on Jan. 26, 2017; Nov. 29, 2022>

Article 110: Deleted. <Jul. 19, 2016>



Article 110-2: (Designation of Special Street Zones)
(1) “Streets prescribed by Presidential Decree” in Article 77-2 (1) of the Act means:
1. A road adjacent to a site, the building line of which is set backed, which is prescribed by a building
ordinance by the relevant permitting authority (referring to the Special Metropolitan City Mayor or a
Metropolitan City Mayor if the permitting authority is a head of a Gu; hereafter in this Article the same
shall apply);
2. A road in an area designated and publicly announced by the relevant permitting authority, as deemed
necessary to promote remodeling therein;
3. A pedestrian-only road prescribed by a building ordinance by the permitting authority to improve a
cityscape;
4. A road in a cultural zone designated under Article 18 of the Regional Culture Promotion Act;

5. Other roads publicly notified by the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport or prescribed by a
building ordinance by the permitting authority to create a balanced cityscape.
(2) "Matters prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 77-2 (2) 4 of the Act means the following
matters:
1. Matters concerning the provisions of this Act or other relevant statutes or regulations not applicable
to, or relaxed for, special street zones and the scope of such relaxed provisions;
2. Matters concerning shapes or colors of the roofs and exterior walls of buildings;
3. Matters concerning building arrangement, and locations of entrances to the sites, and landscaping;
4. Matters concerning the management of the building line setback spaces, POPS, etc.;
5. Other matters publicly notified by the Minister of Land, Infrastructure and Transport or prescribed by
the permitting authority by a building ordinance, as deemed necessary to designate special street zones.



CHAPTER VIII-2 CONSTRUCTION AGREEMENTS



Article 110-3: (Conclusion of Construction Agreements)

“Persons prescribed by Presidential Decree, including the owners of land or buildings and persons with
superficies” in the provisions, with the exception of the subparagraphs, Article 77-4 (1) of the Act, means
the following persons:
1. Owners of land or buildings (including co-owners; hereafter in this paragraph the same shall apply);
2. Persons with superficies of land or buildings;
3. Other persons prescribed by a building ordinance, who have obtained consent from the owners of
land or buildings, among persons who have interests in the said land or buildings.
(2) "Matters prescribed by Presidential Decree" in Article 77-4 (4) 2 of the Act means the following
matters:
1. Building lines;
2. Locations of the relevant building and building service;
3. Use, height, and number of floors of the relevant building;
4. Shapes of the roof and exterior walls of the relevant building;
5. Building-to-land ratio and floor area ratio;
6. Locations and shapes of appurtenant facilities, such as fences, front doors, landscaping, and parking
lots;
7. Shapes of facilities attached to the relevant building, such as a shade or screen facilities;
8. Structures and shapes of party walls referred to in Article 59 (1) 1 of the Act;
9. Other matters prescribed by a building ordinance regarding locations, purposes and shapes of the
relevant building and appurtenant facilities.


<2016. 5. 17.>]

Article 110-4: (Period for Restriction on Annulment of Construction Agreements)
(1) "Period prescribed by Presidential Decree" in the proviso of Article 77-9 (1) of the Act means 20 years
from the filing date of the report on the commencement of the construction works.

(2) Where all of the following requirements are met, the period referred to in paragraph (1) shall be
deemed to have passed, notwithstanding paragraph (1):
1. A site partitioned into pieces under Article 57 (3) of the Act shall be made compliant with the
standards prescribed in paragraphs (1) and (2) of that Act;
2. Authorization for change of a construction agreement shall be obtained with the content that it shall
not be subject to the application of the special provisions prescribed in Article 77-13 of the Act and the
building permission shall be obtained in accordance therewith: Provided, That where approval for use
has been obtained with the content to which the special provisions prescribed in Article 77-13 of the Act
has been applied, the authorization for change of a construction agreement shall be obtained with the
content that it shall not be subject to the application of the special provisions, obtain the building
permission in accordance therewith, and thereafter approval for use of the relevant building shall be
obtained;
3. The project expenses received as a subsidy under Article 77-11 (2) of the Act shall be returned.
[Previous Article 110-4 Moved to Article 110-5 <May 17, 2016>]


<2016. 5. 17.>]

Article 110-5: (Activities to Be Done Pursuant to Construction Agreements)
“Activity prescribed by Presidential Decree” in Article 77-10 (1) of the Act, means any activity related to
the matters referred to in the subparagraphs of Article 110-3 (2).
[Moved from Article 110-4; previous Article 110-5 moved to Article 110-6 <May 17, 2016>]


<2016. 5. 17.>]

Article 110-6: (Support for Construction Agreements)
A person who has the right to authorize construction agreements under Article 77-4 (1) 4 of the Act, may
request a project plan containing the following matters from persons who have concluded a construction
agreement pursuant to Article 77-4 (1) and (2) of the Act (hereinafter referred to as “parties to the
agreement”), or the representative of a construction agreement operations committee established under
Article 77-5: (1) of the Act (hereinafter referred to as “construction agreement operations committee”),
when he or she intends to grant subsidies to cover expenses incurred in a residential environment
improvement project in any construction agreement zone pursuant to Article 77-11 (2) of the Act:
1. Goals of the residential environment improvement project;
2. Names of the parties to the agreement or the representative of the construction agreement operations
committee;
3. Details, and methods of implementation of the residential environment improvement project;
4. Expenses incurred in the residential environment improvement project;
5. Other matters prescribed by a building ordinance.
[Moved from Article 110-5 <May 17, 2016>]



Article 110-7: (Special Cases concerning Construction Agreements)
(1) Pursuant to Article 77-13 (6) of the Act, Articles 42, 55, 56, 60, and 61 of the Act may be relaxed to
apply them to a building to be constructed in a construction agreement zones, according to the following
classification:
1. Landscaping area of a site prescribed in Article 42 of the Act: Limiting to a construction agreement
zone where landscaping of sites is to be conducted en bloc adjoining a road, it may be relaxed within
the limit of 20/100 of the standard landscaping area applicable to the relevant area;
2. Building-to-land ratio prescribed in Article 55 of the Act: It may be relaxed within the limit of 20/100
of the building-to-land ratio applicable to the relevant area. In such cases, the relaxed building-to-land
ratio shall not exceed the maximum limits on the building-to-land ratios prescribed in Article 77 of the
National Land Planning and Utilization Act;
3. Floor area ratio prescribed in Article 56 of the Act: It may be relaxed within the limit of 20/100 of the
floor area ratio applicable to the relevant area. In such cases, the relaxed floor area ratio shall not exceed
the maximum limits on the floor area ratios prescribed in Article 78 of the National Land Planning and
Utilization Act;
4. Limits on heights prescribed in Article 60 of the Act: Limiting to a construction agreement zone
adjoining a road at least six meters wide, it may be relaxed within the limit of 20/100 of the height
standard applicable to the relevant building;
5. Limits on heights of buildings for solar access, etc. prescribed in Article 61 of the Act: Limiting to
multi-family housing to be constructed on both sites within a construction agreement zone, it may be
relaxed within the limit of 20/100 of the standard prescribed in Article 86 (3) 1.
(2) Where the permitting authority intends to conduct consolidated deliberation of the building committee
under Article 4 of the Act and the local urban planning committee under Article 113 of the National Land

Planning and Utilization Act pursuant to the proviso of Article 77-13 (6) of the Act, it shall organize a
consolidated deliberative committee (hereinafter referred to as a "consolidated deliberative committee") in
compliance with the following standards:
1. Members of the consolidated deliberative committee shall be appointed or commissioned by the
Mayor/Do Governor or the head of the Si/Gun/Gu from among members of the building committee
under Article 4 of the Act and the local urban planning committee under Article 113 of the National
Land Planning and Utilization Act;
2. Number of members of the consolidated deliberative committee shall not exceed 15 persons;
3. Number of members of the building committee under Article 4 of the Act shall be at least 1/2 of the
number of members of the consolidated deliberative committee;
4. The chairperson of the consolidated deliberative committee shall be appointed or commissioned by
the Mayor/Do Governor or the head of the Si/Gun/Gu from among the members of the consolidated
deliberative committee.
(3) The consolidated deliberative committee organized under paragraph (2) shall examine the following
matters:
1. Status of land use of the relevant site, and the adequacy of the floor area ratio to be relaxed;
2. Effects of the floor area ratio relaxed by the construction agreement on the surrounding scenery and
environment.
