ADDENDA <Presidential Decree No. 27832, Feb. 3, 2017>
Article 1: (Enforcement Date)
This Decree shall enter into force on February 4, 2017.
Article 2: (Applicability to Relaxed Application of Criteria to Buildings)
The amended provision of Article 6 (1) 6 (c) shall begin to apply from the first application for building
permission or permission for substantial repair filed pursuant to Article 11 of the Act (including an

application for deliberation filed with a building committee pursuant to Article 4-2 of the Act to apply
for building permission or a permission for substantial repair) or the first notification of building
construction filed pursuant to Article 14 of the Act, after this Decree enters into force.
Article 3: (Transitional Measures concerning Submission of Documents Verifying Structural Safety)
Notwithstanding the amended provision of Article 32 (2) 1, the previous provisions shall apply to the
submission of documents certifying structural safety related to the relevant construction, substantial
repair, or change of use in any of the following cases:
1. Where building permission or permission for substantial repair under Article 11 of the Act, a
notification of building construction under Article 14 of the Act, or permission for, or a report on,
change of use under Article 19 of the Act is received or accepted, before this Decree enters into force;
2. Where an application for building permission or permission for substantial repair under Article 11 of
the Act (including an application for deliberation filed with a building committee pursuant to Article 4-
2 of the Act to apply for building permission or permission for substantial repair), a notification of
building construction under Article 14 of the Act, an application for permission for, or a report on,
change of use under Article 19 of the Act is filed, before this Decree enters into force;
3. Where permission for alteration is received or a notification of change is filed with respect to
building permission, permission for substantial repair, or a notification of building construction,
received or accepted pursuant to subparagraph 1 or 2, after this Decree enters into force.
Article 4: Omitted.

ADDENDA <Presidential Decree No. 30624, Apr. 21, 2020>
Article 1: (Enforcement Date)
This Act shall enter into force six months after the date of its promulgation: Provided, That the amended
provisions of Article 115 shall enter into force on April 24, 2020.
Article 2: (Applicability to Project Supervision)
The amended provisions of Article 19 (6) shall begin to apply where a report on the commencement of
construction works is filed under Article 21 of the Act, after this Decree enters into force.

Article 3: (Applicability to Interior Construction)
The amended provisions of subparagraph 3 of Article 61-2 shall also apply to buildings whose interior
construction is performed before this Decree enters into force. In such cases, it shall conform to the
standards concerning the structure, execution method, etc. of interior construction under Article 52-2 (2)
of the Act within one year from the enforcement date of this Decree.
Article 4: (Applicability to Calculation of Building-to-Land Ratio)
The amended provisions of Article 119 (3) shall begin to apply where there is a filing of an application
for building permission under Article 11 of the Act (including an application for deliberation by a
building committee under Article 4-2 (1) of the Act to apply for permission), or a notification of
building construction filed under Article 14 of the Act, after this Decree enters into force.
Article 5: (Transitional Measures concerning Deliberation by Local Building Committees)
Notwithstanding the amended provisions of Article 5-5 (1) 6, 8, and (6) 2 (i), the previous provisions
shall apply to an application for deliberation filed with a local building committee under Article 4-2 (1)
of the Act before this Decree enters into force.

Article 1: (Enforcement Date)
This Decree shall enter into force on October 8, 2020: Provided, That the following amended provisions
shall enter into force on the dates specified as follows:
1. The amended provisions of Articles 15 (6) 1 (a), 46 (2) 3, 51 (2) 2 (c), and 53 (1) 3 through 6: Six
months after the date of its promulgation;
2. The amended provisions of Articles 46 (1), 46 (4) 4 and 5, 62 (1) 3, and 64 of the Enforcement
Decree of the Presidential Decree No. 30030: August 7, 2021;
3. The amended provisions of Article 61 (1) (excluding subparagraph 3 of the same paragraph): Three
months after the date of its promulgation.

The amended provisions of Article 61 (1) 6 shall begin to apply where there is a filing of an application
for building permission under Article 11 of the Act (including an application for deliberation by a
building  committee  filed  under  Article  4-2  (1)  of  the  Act  to  apply  for  building  permission);  a
notification of building construction under Article 14 of the Act; or an application for permission to
change of use under Article 19 of the Act (including a report on change of use or an application for
alteration of the entries in the building register filed under the same Article), after the amended
provisions enter into force under subparagraph 1 of Article 1 of the Addenda.
1. The amended provisions of Articles 46 (1) 4, 62 (1) 3 and 64 of the Enforcement Decree of the
partially  amended  Decree  of  the  Enforcement  Decree  No.  30030,  and  the  partially  amended
Enforcement Decree of the Decree of the Decree: The enforcement date under subparagraph 2 of Article
1 of the Addenda;

subparagraph 1 of Article 1 of the Addenda;
3. The amended provisions of Articles 51 (2) 2 (c) and 53 (1) 3 concerning postnatal care centers: the
enforcement date under subparagraph 1 of Article 1 of the Addenda;
4. Amended provisions of Article 61 (1) (excluding subparagraph 3 of the same paragraph) concerning
interior finishing materials for buildings: Enforcement date under subparagraph 3 of Article 1 of the
Addenda.
Article 3: (Applicability to Construction of Temporary Buildings)
The amended provisions of Article 15 (6) 1 (a) shall begin to apply where there is a filing of an
application for building permission or report on construction of a temporary building referred to in
Article 15: (5) 2 or 14 after the enforcement date prescribed in subparagraph 1 of Article 1 of the
Addenda.
Article 4: (Transitional Measures concerning Imposition of Administrative Fines)
The disposition of an administrative fine imposed for a violation committed before this Presidential
Decree enters into force shall be included in calculation of the number of violations pursuant to the
amended provisions of item (d) of subparagraph 2 of Appendix 16.
Article 5: Omitted.

building construction under Article 14 of the Act; or an application for permission to change of use

under Article 19 of the Act (including a report on change of use or an application for alteration of the
entries in the building register under the same Article), after the amended provisions enter into force as
follows:
1. The amended provisions of Article 61 (3) concerning buildings requiring the installation of windows
and doors having fireproofing performance: June 23, 2021;
2. The amended provisions of subparagraphs 3 (j) and 20 (i) of Appendix 1 concerning Class 1
neighborhood living facilities: The date of its promulgation.
3. The amended provisions of subparagraph 4 (p) (ii) of Appendix 1 concerning Class 2 neighborhood
living facilities: The date of its promulgation.


<31941, 2021. 8. 10.>



ADDENDA <Presidential Decree No. 31941, Aug. 10, 2021>
Article 1: (Enforcement Date)
This Decree shall enter into force six months after the date of its promulgation: Provided, That the
amended  provisions  of  Article  46  (5)  4  shall  enter  into  force  one  month  after  the  date  of  the

promulgation.
Article 2: (Applicability to Placement of Assistant Architects for Installation of Finishing Materials)
The amended provisions of Article 19 (7) shall begin to apply where supervision services are provided
for the installation of finishing materials for a building for which the following application or report is
filed after this Decree enters into force:
1. An application for building permission (excluding permission for changes and a report on changes
under Article 16 of the Act) under Article 11 of the Act (including where an application for deliberation
of a building committee is filed pursuant to Article 4-2 (1) of the Act to apply for building permission);
2. A notification of building construction under Article 14 of the Act (excluding permission for or
reports on changes under Article 16 of the Act);
3. An application for permission for the change of use under Article 19 of the Act (including reports on
the change of use of a building or applications for the change of entries in the building register under the
same paragraph).
Article 3: (Applicability to Buildings Requiring Use of Fireproof Interior Finishing Materials)
The amended provisions of Article 61 (1) 4 shall begin to apply where interior finishing materials are
installed for a building for which an application or report is filed under the subparagraphs of Article 2 of
Addenda after this Decree enters into force.
Article 4: (Applicability to Buildings Requiring Use of Fireproof Finishing Materials on Exterior
Walls)
The amended provisions of Article 61 (2) 5 shall begin to apply where finishing materials are installed
on the exterior walls of a building for which an application or report is filed under the subparagraphs of
Article 2: of the Addenda after this Decree enters into force.
Article 5: Omitted.

<32102, 2021. 11. 2.>



ADDENDA <Presidential Decree No. 32102, Nov. 2, 2021>
Article 1: (Enforcement Date)
This  Decree  shall  enter  into  force  on  the  date  of  its  promulgation:  Provided,  That  the  amended
provisions  of  Article  15  (7)  shall  enter  into  force  six  months  after  the  date  of  its  promulgation.
Article 2: (Applicability to Calculation of Area)
The amended provisions of Article 119 (1) 2 (a) (vi) shall begin to apply to a building, for which any of
the following applications or reports is filed after this Decree enters into force:
1. An application for building permission (including permission for or a report on changes under Article
16 of the Act) under Article 11 of the Act (including where an application for deliberation by a building

committee  is  filed  pursuant  to  Article  4-2  (1)  of  the  Act  for  purposes  of  applying  for  building
permission);
2. A notification of building construction under Article 14 of the Act (including permission for or a
report on changes under Article 16 of the Act);
3. An application for permission for the change of use under Article 19 of the Act (including reports on
the change of use of a building or applications for the change of entries in the building register under
that Article).
Article 3: (Applicability to Requirements for Living Lodging Facilities)
The amended provisions of subparagraph 15 (a) of Appendix 1 shall begin to apply to living lodging
facilities for which an application or a report referred to in the subparagraphs of Article 2 of the
Addenda is filed after this Decree enters into force.
Article 4: (Transitional Measures concerning Extension of Retention Period of Temporary Buildings)
Notwithstanding the amended provisions of Article 15 (7), the previous provisions shall apply to the
extension of the retention period of a temporary building, the construction of which has been reported
under Article 20 (3) of the Act before this Decree enters into force.
Article 5: (Transitional Measures concerning Distance for Ensuring Daylight Availability for Multi-
Family Housing)
(1) A local government shall enact or amend a building ordinance under the amended provisions of
Article 86: (3) 2 (b) no later than six months after the date this Decree enters into force.
(2) The previous building ordinance shall apply until a new building ordinance is enacted or amended
pursuant to paragraph (1).
(3)  The  distance  standard  (referring  to  the  lower  limit  of  the  distance  prescribed  by  a  building
ordinance) under the amended provisions of Article 86 (3) 2 (b) shall apply to the distance for ensuring
daylight availability for multi-family housing where a building ordinance is not enacted or amended by
the deadline under paragraph (1).

<32614, 2022. 4. 29.>



ADDENDA <Presidential Decree No. 32614, Apr. 29, 2022>
Article 1: (Enforcement Date)
This Decree shall enter into force on the date of its promulgation.
Article 2: (Transitional  Measures  concerning  Part  of  Building  Need  Not  Be  Partitioned  as  Fire
Compartment)
Notwithstanding the amended provisions of Article 46 (2) 2, the previous provisions shall apply to the
duty  to  install  a  fire  compartment  for  part  of  a  building  falling  under  any  of  the  following
subparagraphs:
1. A building, for which building permission or permission for substantial repair (including permission
for or reporting on change under Article 16) pursuant to Article 11 of the Act has been obtained or
applied for (including where an application for deliberation by a building committee has been filed
under Article 4-2 (1) of the Act for purposes of applying for building permission or permission for
substantial repair) before this Decree enters into force;
2. A building, for which the notification of building construction under Article 14 of the Act (including
permission for or reporting on change under Article 16 of the Act) has been filed before this Decree
enters into force;
3. A building, for which permission for change of use under Article 19 of the Act (including reports on
the change of use and applications for the modification of entries in the building register under that
Article) or an application therefor has been obtained or filed before this Decree enters into force.

<33249, 2023. 2. 14.>



ADDENDA <Presidential Decree No. 33249, Feb. 14, 2023>
Article 1: (Enforcement Date)
This Act shall enter into force on the date of its promulgation.
Article 2: (Applicability to Requirements for Dormitories)
The amended provisions, with the exception of subparagraph 2 (d) (i) and (ii), of Appendix 1 shall
begin to apply where the following applications or reports are filed after the date this Decree enters into
force:
1. An application for building permission (including where an application for deliberation by a building
committee is filed under Article 4-2 (1) of the Act to apply for building permission) under Article 11 of
the Act;
2. A notification of building construction under Article 14 of the Act;
3. An application for permission for the change of use under Article 19 of the Act (including reports on
the change of use of a building or applications for the change of entries in the building register under
that paragraph);
4. An application for, or report on, permission, authorization, approval, etc. under other statutes by
which it is deemed that permission is granted or a report is filed under subparagraphs 1 through 3.

Article 3: (Transitional Measures concerning Classification of Uses of Existing Dormitories)
(1)  A  building  for  a  use  corresponding  to  a  dormitory  referred  to  in  the  previous  provisions  of
subparagraph 2 (d) of Appendix 1, as at the time this Decree enters into force, shall be deemed a
building for a use corresponding to a general dormitory referred to in the amended provisions of
subparagraph 2 (d) (i) of Appendix 1.
(2) Where an application or report prescribed in the subparagraphs of Article 2 of the Addenda is filed
for the use as a dormitory under the previous provisions of subparagraph 2 (d) of Appendix 1 before this
Decree enters into force, such application or report shall be deemed to have been filed for the use as a
general dormitory under the amended provisions of subparagraph 2 (d) (i) of Appendix 1.

<33466, 2023. 5. 15.>




ADDENDA <Presidential Decree No. 33466, May 15, 2023>
Article 1: (Enforcement Date)
This Decree shall enter into force on May 16, 2023.
Article 2: (Transitional Measures concerning Classification of Uses of Existing Correctional or Military
Facilities)
(1)  A  building  for  a  use  corresponding  to  a  correctional  or  military  facility  under  the  previous
provisions of subparagraph 23 (excluding item (d)) of Appendix 1 as at the time this Decree enters into
force shall be deemed a building for a use corresponding to a correctional facility under the amended
provisions of subparagraph 23 of Appendix 1.
(2) A building for a use corresponding to a defense or military facility under the previous provisions of
subparagraph 23 (d) of Appendix 1, as at the time this Decree enters into force, shall be deemed a
building for a use corresponding to a defense or military facility under the amended provisions of
subparagraph 23-2 of Appendix 1.
Article 3: Omitted.


<33717, 2023. 9. 12.>



ADDENDA <Presidential Decree No. 33717, Sep. 12, 2023>
Article 1: (Enforcement Date)
This Decree shall enter into force on the date of its promulgation: Provided, That any of the following
matters shall enter into force on the dates classified as follows:
1. The amended provisions of Article 19 (11) through (13): The date six months elapse after the date of
its promulgation;
2. The amended provisions of Article 119 (1) 3 (o): The date one year elapses after the date of its
promulgation.
Article 2: (Applicability to Installation of Refuge Areas)
The amended provisions of Article 46 (4) and (5) shall begin to apply to the following applications or
reports filed after the date this Decree enters into force:
1. An application for building permission (including permission for or a report on changes under Article
16 of the Act) under Article 11 of the Act (including where an application for deliberation by a building
committee is filed pursuant to Article 4-2 (1) of the Act to apply for building permission);

2. A notification of building construction under Article 14 of the Act (including permission for or a
report on changes under Article 16 of the Act);
3. An application for, or report on, permission, authorization, approval, etc. under other statutes by
which it is deemed that permission is granted or a report is filed under subparagraphs 1 and 2.
Article 3: (Applicability to Restrictions on Height of Buildings for Solar Access)
The amended provisions of the subparagraphs of Article 86 (1) shall begin to apply to applications or
reports filed under the subparagraphs of Article 2 of the Addenda after a building ordinance is enacted
or amended under the main clause of that paragraph.
Article 4: (Applicability to Standards for Calculation of Floor Area of Refuge Areas)
The amended provisions of Article 119 (1) 3 (o) shall begin to apply applications or reports filed after
the enforcement date under subparagraph 2 of Article 1 of the Addenda:
1. An application for building permission (excluding permission for changes and a report on changes
under Article 16 of the Act) under Article 11 of the Act (including where an application for deliberation
of a building committee is filed under Article 4-2 (1) of the Act to apply for building permission);
2. A notification of building construction under Article 14 of the Act (excluding permission for or
reports on changes under Article 16 of the Act);
3. An application for, or report on, permission, authorization, approval, etc. under other statutes by
which it is deemed that permission is granted or a report is filed under subparagraphs 1 and 2.
Article 5: (Applicability to Exclusion of Floor Area from Calculation)
The amended provisions of Article 19 (1) 3 (p) shall begin to apply to applications or reports filed under
the subparagraphs of Article 2 of the Addenda after the date this Decree enters into force.
Article 6: (Applicability to Classification of Use of Animal Hospitals)
The amended provisions of subparagraph 3 (k) of Appendix 1 and subparagraph 4 (j) of that Table shall
begin to apply where the following applications or reports are filed after the date this Decree enters into
force:
1. An application for building permission (excluding permission for changes and a report on changes
under Article 16 of the Act) under Article 11 of the Act (including where an application for deliberation
of a building committee is filed under Article 4-2 (1) of the Act to apply for building permission);
2. A notification of building construction under Article 14 of the Act (excluding permission for or
reports on changes under Article 16 of the Act);
3. An application for permission for the change of use under Article 19 of the Act (including reports on
the change of use of a building or applications for the change of entries in the building register under
that paragraph);
4. An application for, or report on, permission, authorization, approval, etc. under other statutes by
which it is deemed that permission is granted or a report is filed under subparagraphs 1 and 2.
